Admin guide and CLAUDE.md no longer make claims contradicted by code.

3. **Saved-search JSON schema validation on restore**
   - **Description:** Replace the bare `JSON.parse` + typed cast in `SavedSearchList.tsx:76,163` (and the same pattern in `SearchCollections.tsx`) with a runtime validator (zod schema or hand-rolled type guard) for `IActiveFilter[]`, `IHistoryStateSummary`, and the persisted `searchState` shape. On validation failure, surface a Fluent `MessageBar` "This saved search uses an unrecognized format and cannot be restored" and skip the apply-to-store step. Closes SEC-004.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (b) security — a tampered saved search shared between users can poison the store with no UI signal (Appendix A SEC-004 Still-Open). ##### Coverage walk (spec §4.3 T2 scope item → mapping)

- **Saved searches** → D3 (validation), D6 (library boundary), D10 (save flow polish)
- **Collections / pinboards** → D4 (Comments on collection items), D6 (library toggle)
- **Sharing** → D1 (notification), D5 (ManageAccess), D10c (unsaved-share path)
- **History** → D8 (Back/Forward integration covers query history); retention TTL config is Out of Scope (admin-track concern)
- **Annotations** → D4 (Comments extension to existing tag editor)
- **Keyboard shortcuts** → D9 (global shortcut layer + help dialog)
- **Multi-select bulk actions** → D2 (wire BulkActionsToolbar)
- **Export (CSV today, XLSX deferred)** → D11 (layout-agnostic export — XLSX already shipped per MISS-003 Closed)
- **Comments component integration** → D4
- **Recent + trending suggestions** → D13 (interim rename) + Out of Scope (org-wide aggregation deferred to v1.1)
- **Query templates** → Out of Scope (defer to v1.1; no shipped surface today)
- **Personal vs shared library boundaries** → D5 (ManageAccess), D6 (Owned/Shared-with-me toggle)

#### Out of scope for v1.0

- **Graph mail send + Activity Feed posts on share.** Rationale: D1 covers in-product notification (the actual Blocker fix) without the Graph permissions overhead. Mail send adds `Mail.Send` consent + delivery-failure surface; Activity Feed (`/me/insights/used`) requires per-tenant configuration. Capture as v1.1 once D1's notification model proves out.
- **End-user-defined query templates.** Rationale: Spec §4.3 T2 scope item but no shipped surface today, no journey friction logged, and saved searches already cover the most common parameterized-query use case. Net-new feature work, not productivity polish — defer to v1.1 after observing how saved-search categories are used in the wild.
- **History retention TTL property pane configuration.** Rationale: Journey A Step 10 [Confusion] tagged this Foundations / T4 (admin-configurable retention) at `:142`. T2 owns the *user-visible* history surface (D8 Back/Forward); the admin-configurable retention window is captured under T4 and Foundations stale-docs deliverables, not T2.
- **ConflictDetector adoption on saved-search and collection edits.** Rationale: Appendix B ConflictDetector (Consider) classes ConflictDetector as `Consider` not `Adopt`, and the qualifier "worthwhile only if user research shows real concurrent-edit pain" is explicit. No journey friction logged on concurrent edit. Optimistic-overwrite default is acceptable for v1.0; revisit in v1.1 if user research surfaces the issue.
- **Real-time history surfaces (replace polling with WebSocket / Graph subscriptions).** Rationale: D1 polling notification is sufficient for v1.0 ship; Microsoft Graph change notifications add tenant-config + AAD subscription overhead that exceeds the "self-serve any tenant" audience profile. Defer to v1.1.
- **Shareable search "rooms" / multi-user collaborative sessions.** Rationale: out of audience-profile scope ("self-serve any tenant"); requires real-time presence + conflict resolution + a tenant-shared backend. Different product shape entirely; not v1.0 polish.
- **Drag-and-drop reordering of saved searches and collection items.** Rationale: existing alphabetical / category grouping covers the use case; HTML5 DnD adds keyboard-a11y complexity (custom `aria-grabbed` + screen reader announcements) for marginal lift. Post-launch polish.

### T3. Multi-Instance / Multi-Context

#### Current state

T3 is the project's strongest differentiator versus PnP Modern Search v4 — PnP has no multi-context model at all (Appendix C "Multi-instance isolation via `searchContextId`" — "PnP v4 uses Dynamic Data which couples instances"). The implementation rests on three deliberate architectural choices: a window-backed singleton context map that survives webpack entry-point duplication, a stable per-context URL prefix computed at context creation, and a per-vertical `dataProviderId` field that lets one context route different verticals to different providers. The substrate is real, but the surface area exposed to admins and end users is thin in three places: collision detection, lifecycle cleanup, and URL alias namespacing.

The actual T3 surface, by file:

- **`searchContextId` correctness.** Every web part declares `searchContextId: string` with manifest default `"default"` (`SpSearchBoxWebPart.manifest.json:25`, `SpSearchResultsWebPart.manifest.json:25`, `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.manifest.json:25`, `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.manifest.json:25`, `SpSearchManagerWebPart.manifest.json:25`, `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.manifest.json:18`). Each web part normalizes via `this.properties.searchContextId || 'default'` (e.g. `SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:129`, `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:153,189`, `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:91`, `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:121`, `SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:139`). All web parts re-resolve the store when the property changes (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:852-856`, `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:200-204`, `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:234-237`).
- **URL parameter namespacing.** `urlSyncMiddleware.ts:79-81` defines `prefixKey(key, prefix)` which produces `{prefix}.{key}` when prefix is set. Reserved param keys (`q`, `v`, `s`, `p`, `l`, `x`, `i`) and filter aliases all flow through this path (`urlSyncMiddleware.ts:87-95, 97-99, 105-113`). The prefix itself is computed deterministically at context creation via `_buildStableUrlPrefix(searchContextId)` (`storeRegistry.ts:217, 292-306`) — a normalized 6-char stem + 6-char FNV-1a hex hash, stable across reloads. `pushStateToUrl` debounce timers are keyed per-prefix (`urlSyncMiddleware.ts:586-593`), so two contexts cannot stomp each other's pending URL writes.
- **Per-vertical `dataProviderId` routing.** `IVerticalDefinition.ts:16` declares `dataProviderId?: string`. `SearchOrchestrator._getProvider(state)` (`SearchOrchestrator.ts:544-557`) reads the active vertical and prefers a provider matching `vertical.dataProviderId`, falling back to the first registered provider. `Provision-TestPages.ps1:354-380` exercises this path with the `multi-people` context routing the People vertical to Graph while Documents stays on SharePoint Search.
- **Cross-context coordination.** Each context owns a separate `ISearchContext` (`storeRegistry.ts:18-26`) with its own store, orchestrator, registries, and URL sync subscription. There is no cross-context publish/subscribe API; coordination is intentionally absent so isolation is the default contract.
- **Library-component singleton backing.** `storeRegistry.ts:36-54` stores both `__sp_search_context_map__` and `__sp_search_init_promises__` on `window` to defeat webpack entry-point duplication. Without this, every web part bundle would receive its own module-scoped Map and "shared" contexts would in fact be N independent stores — the failure mode SP Search exists to prevent. The init-promises map (`storeRegistry.ts:119-138`) serializes concurrent `initializeSearchContext()` calls so two web parts racing to bootstrap the same context resolve once.
- **Multi-context URL prefix race repair.** `storeRegistry.ts:224-234` re-subscribes ALL previously-initialized contexts when `map.size` transitions from 1 to 2, so the first-loaded context picks up its stable prefix mid-session (BUG-005 Closed in Appendix A; `storeRegistry.ts:217` computes the prefix at context creation rather than at first URL write).
- **Sample multi-context pages.** `scripts/Provision-TestPages.ps1:319-381` provisions `test-multi-context` with two independent contexts (`multi-docs`, `multi-people`) — Search Box + Results + Filters per context, scenario-preset-tuned, on one page. No documentation page exists today (`docs/admin-guide.md` mentions multi-context only in passing at `:3` and lists `searchContextId` in the per-web-part property tables; `docs/extensibility-guide.md:9, 537-552` documents the registry pattern but ships no walkthrough or screenshots).
- **Edit-mode default-context advisory.** `SpSearchResults.tsx:716-720` renders an edit-only `MessageBar` when `searchContextId === 'default'`. This is the only in-product hint that multi-context awareness exists. There is **no** detection or warning for the inverse case (Box uses `default`, Results uses `hr-search` — orphaned web parts). There is no edit-mode warning for any of the other five web parts.
- **Property pane discoverability.** The `searchContextId` field lives at inconsistent locations: page 3 of 4 in Search Box (`SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:362-375`), page 3 of 4 in Search Results (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:1207-1228`), page 2 of 3 in Search Filters (`SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:443-463`), **page 1 group 1** in Verticals (`SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:317-330`), and page 1 group 1 in Manager (`SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:201-215`). Three distinct description strings ship across the five web parts (`spSearchBox/loc/en-us.js:17`, `spSearchResults/loc/en-us.js:17`, `spSearchFilters/loc/en-us.js:14`).
- **Filter URL alias collision risk.** `filterUrlAliases.ts:18-46` maps short codes (`au`, `md`, `ft`, `ct`, `ti`, `pa`, `sz`, `cr`, `cc`) without uniqueness checks. Two managed properties that normalize to the same alias (e.g. `Author` and `AuthorOWSUSER` both produce `au` per `:18`) collide silently — the second filter's value overwrites the first at URL write time and the wrong filter is restored on deep-link load. The risk amplifies in multi-context pages where each context has its own filter set but shares the same alias namespace shape.
- **Lifecycle / cleanup gap.** `disposeStore(searchContextId)` is exported (`storeRegistry.ts:245-258`), tears down the URL sync subscription, stops the orchestrator, aborts in-flight searches, and removes the context from the map. **It is never called from any web part `onDispose()`** (`grep -rn 'disposeStore' src/webparts` returns 0 hits). Each web part's `onDispose` only unmounts the React tree (`SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:209-213`, `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:840-842`, `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:190-192`, `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:222`, `SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:186-188`). The window-backed map persists across navigation within an SPA shell and across web part re-mount cycles; orchestrators keep running, popstate listeners stay attached, debounce timers stay armed.

Closed/Changed-Form items already in the T3 surface (per Appendix A): BUG-003 (URL filter restore timeout), BUG-005 (multi-context URL prefix race), BUG-009 (scope round-trip), INC-006 (`reset()` aborts AbortController), BUG-006 (Obsolete — debounce stale-state was design intent). Still-Open items in T3's path: ARCH-003 (initialization order dependency not enforced — owning track Foundations but the failure mode lands on T3 multi-context init).

#### Gap to "amazing"

The audience profile is "any SPFx-capable tenant, self-serve, no author hand-holding" — and T3 is the moat. PnP Modern Search v4 has no multi-context concept at all, so a tenant evaluating SP Search alongside PnP needs to see the moat without reading the source. Today four failure modes erode that promise. **First, collision detection is silent in both directions**: the only edit-mode advisory fires when `searchContextId === 'default'` on the Results web part — the inverse case (Results uses `hr-search` while Box and Filters still use `default`, or any pairwise mismatch between connected web parts) shows no warning anywhere, and an admin who mistypes one ID gets a search page where the box and results don't talk to each other with no in-product diagnostic. **Second, lifecycle cleanup is a leak in waiting**: `disposeStore` exists, is correct, and is wired to nothing — so a SharePoint SPA shell navigation away from a search page leaves a context, orchestrator subscription, popstate listener, and debounce timer alive on `window.__sp_search_context_map__` indefinitely; over a long session a single tab accumulates orchestrators, each subscribing to its own (now-invisible) store. **Third, URL alias namespacing has a per-context gap**: short aliases (`au`, `md`, `ft`) are computed deterministically without uniqueness checks, so two managed properties in the same filterConfig that normalize to the same alias collide silently — the second filter's value wins on write, the first vanishes from deep links. The collision space gets denser in multi-context pages because each context owns its own alias namespace shape but admins authoring two contexts side-by-side don't see the shared-alias risk in any property pane validation. **Fourth, the moat is undocumented**: a `test-multi-context` provisioning page exists but there is no admin doc, no walkthrough, no screenshot of the resulting URL (`?ctx1.q=...&ctx2.q=...`), no troubleshooting flowchart. A self-serve admin reading the docs cannot find a single sentence that says "to put two independent searches on one page, set searchContextId to two different values." The architecture protects them; the docs do not advertise it.

#### Deliverables

1. **Wire `disposeStore` into every web part `onDispose` with last-mounted-wins refcounting**
   - **Description:** Add a per-context refcount to `storeRegistry.ts` (`incrementContextRef(searchContextId)` at the end of each web part's `onInit` after `getStore`; `decrementContextRef(searchContextId)` at the start of each web part's `onDispose`; when refcount transitions 1 → 0, call existing `disposeStore(searchContextId)`). The refcount path must defer dispose to a microtask (`queueMicrotask` or `setTimeout 0`) so a new mount with the same `searchContextId` can re-increment first, preventing premature cleanup during SPA cross-page navigation (SharePoint Modern can fire a new page's `onInit` before the old page's `onDispose`); if after the microtask the refcount is still 0, then dispose. Update `SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:209-213`, `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:840-842`, `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:190-192`, `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:222` (`onDispose` method, currently a single line), `SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:186-188`, and `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts` (inherits from Manager — verify single-call semantics) to call `decrementContextRef(this.properties.searchContextId || 'default')` before `ReactDom.unmountComponentAtNode`. Refcount the contextId NOT the WebPart instance so a single page hosting two web parts on the same context drops cleanly when the second web part unmounts. Document the contract on the public `disposeStore` JSDoc (`storeRegistry.ts:241-244`) so library-component consumers (e.g. third-party extensions per `extensibility-guide.md:537-552`) know they must refcount themselves.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (b) security (popstate handler + orchestrator subscription continue firing on unloaded pages can leak prior search state across same-tab SharePoint navigation) and (a) T3 differentiator (the documented `disposeStore` API is currently a no-op on every shipped web part). Required-Scenario S4 (navigation away/back behavior + store cleanup expectations) has no current coverage; this is the deliverable.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** none
   - **Source:** Required scenario S4; Phase 6.3 discovery: `grep -rn 'disposeStore' src/webparts` returns 0 hits while `storeRegistry.ts:245-258` ships a complete dispose path; Appendix A INC-006 (Closed) demonstrates the abort path is in place but never invoked from web part lifecycle
   - **Acceptance signal:** Manual: load a multi-context page, navigate to a second SharePoint page, return — `window.__sp_search_context_map__.size` returns to 0 after the last web part unmounts (verified in DevTools console). Unit test in `tests/store/storeRegistry.test.ts` covers (a) two web parts on one context dispose to 0 only after BOTH unmount, (b) two contexts with two web parts each dispose independently, (c) re-mount after dispose creates a fresh context (no state bleed). `grep -rn 'decrementContextRef\\|disposeStore' src/webparts` returns ≥6 hits (one per web part).

2. **Cross-web-part `searchContextId` mismatch warning in edit mode**
   - **Description:** Extend the existing `SpSearchResults.tsx:716-720` MessageBar pattern with a registry-backed mismatch detector. Add `recordWebPartContextId(componentId: string, instanceId: string, searchContextId: string)` to `storeRegistry.ts` (writes to `window.__sp_search_webpart_registrations__`, populated from each web part's `onInit` with `this.context.manifest.id` + `this.context.instanceId`). In edit mode each web part reads the registration map and renders a Fluent `MessageBar messageBarType={MessageBarType.warning}` when its own `searchContextId` differs from any other registered web part on the page (or when one of: Box, Results, Filters, Verticals is missing while at least one other is present). Surface in all five user-facing web parts (Box, Results, Filters, Verticals, Manager). Copy: "Search Box uses 'default' but Search Results uses 'hr-search' — these web parts are not connected. Set both to the same Search Context ID." Hide in view mode (admin-only diagnostic). On D1's `decrementContextRef` reaching 0 (or per web part dispose, whichever fires first), call `unrecordWebPartContextId(instanceId)` to remove the row from `__sp_search_webpart_registrations__` — otherwise the mismatch detector reports phantom mismatches against unmounted web parts.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T3 differentiator and (e) Journey A Step 7 [Confusion] (mismatch is invisible — no documented workaround other than "open every property pane and read the value yourself"). The current `default`-context advisory only covers the symmetric "everyone is on default" case; the asymmetric case where ONE web part is mistyped is the actual day-1 admin failure mode and has zero in-product detection. Required-Scenario S2 (two web parts accidentally sharing/diverging context ID when isolation was expected) is the inverse case this warning covers.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** none
   - **Source:** Required scenario S2; Journey A Step 7 [Confusion]
   - **Acceptance signal:** Add Search Box + Results to a page; set Box `searchContextId="hr-search"`, leave Results on `default` — both web parts render a warning MessageBar in edit mode listing the conflicting IDs and the affected component names. Set both to `hr-search` — the warning disappears. Switch to view mode — no warning visible to end users. Unit test in `tests/store/contextMismatchDetector.test.ts` covers three IDs across four web parts and asserts the produced warning string.

3. **Filter URL alias uniqueness validation and collision warning**
   - **Description:** In `filterUrlAliases.ts:49-51` (`getFilterUrlAlias`) add a uniqueness check across the active `filterConfig`: if two filters resolve to the same alias, append a 2-char hash suffix to the second + nth occurrences (e.g. `au-7c`, `au-3f`) computed via the existing `_stableHash` pattern (`storeRegistry.ts:299-306`). Log a `console.warn` once per unique collision and surface a Fluent edit-mode `MessageBar` on the Filters web part listing collided pairs. Update the `IFilterConfig.urlAlias` property pane row in `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts` to show "auto" or the collision-derived alias inline. Document the policy in the JSDoc of `getFilterUrlAlias` (`:49`) and in `docs/admin-guide.md` per the Deliverable 5 docs page.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T3 differentiator and (c) data integrity. Required-Scenario S3 covers URL deep-link parameters for two contexts — collision risk applies per-context AND across contexts (in multi-context pages each context still draws from the same alias generator). The current silent overwrite at deep-link restore time produces "wrong filter applied" with no signal anywhere in the journey.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** none
   - **Source:** Required scenario S3; Journey B Step 11 [Confusion]; Phase 6.3 discovery: `filterUrlAliases.ts:18-46` has no uniqueness check across `getDefaultFilterUrlAlias` outputs; `Author` + `AuthorOWSUSER` both normalize to `au`
   - **Acceptance signal:** Configure Filters web part with `Author` + `AuthorOWSUSER` simultaneously — edit-mode MessageBar lists the collision and the chosen disambiguated alias for the second filter; URL deep link with both filters round-trips correctly (each filter restores to its original managed property). Unit test in `tests/utils/filterUrlAliases.test.ts` covers (a) no collision → original alias, (b) two-property collision → `au` + `au-{hash}`, (c) three-property collision → `au` + `au-{h1}` + `au-{h2}`.

   - **Description:** Move the `PropertyPaneTextField('searchContextId', ...)` block to page 1 group 1 in every web part: `SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:362-375` (currently page 3), `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:1207-1228` (currently page 3), `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:443-463` (currently page 2), `SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:201-215` (already page 1, verify position), `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts` (inherits from Manager). 6. **Per-context URL prefix opt-out and explicit-prefix override property**
   - **Description:** Today the URL prefix is auto-computed from `searchContextId` and only activates when `getContextMap().size > 1` (`storeRegistry.ts:176`). Add an admin-facing override: extend `IPropertyPaneSearchContextIdOptions` (the helper introduced in D4) with an optional `urlPrefix` property pane field (e.g. `?ctx1.q=...` instead of `?defauld87fe2.q=...`). When provided, the explicit prefix wins over `_buildStableUrlPrefix(searchContextId)` (`storeRegistry.ts:217, 292-297`). Also expose `enableUrlSync: boolean` (default `true`) so an admin can opt a context out of URL sync entirely (useful for embedded "saved-search runner" widgets that must not stomp the page URL). Wire both into the existing `createUrlSyncSubscription` factory (`urlSyncMiddleware.ts:665-783`) — when `enableUrlSync === false`, return the existing SSR no-op unsubscribe path.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T3 differentiator. Required-Scenario S3 (URL deep-link parameters for two contexts on the same page) ships today with auto-computed 6+6-char prefixes that produce ugly URLs (`?defauld87fe2.q=annual+report&peopl4f3a91.q=john`). Admins running side-by-side contexts want short readable prefixes (`?ctx1.q=...&ctx2.q=...`), and embedders running headless contexts want URL-sync-off entirely. Both are quality-of-life improvements that compound with D5's documentation walkthrough.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 4 (shared property pane helper is the natural home for the new fields)
   - **Source:** Required scenario S3; spec §4.3 T3 explicit scope item ("URL parameter namespacing (`?ctx1.q=...`)"); Phase 6.3 discovery: `_buildStableUrlPrefix` (`storeRegistry.ts:292-297`) produces normalized 6-char stem + 6-char hash with no admin override path
   - **Acceptance signal:** Admin sets `urlPrefix: "ctx1"` on Context A and `urlPrefix: "ctx2"` on Context B — typing in both search boxes produces `?ctx1.q=annual&ctx2.q=john`. Setting `enableUrlSync: false` on a single-context embedded widget — the URL stays clean while the in-page search still works. Unit test in `tests/middleware/urlSync.test.ts` asserts both override paths.

7. **Per-vertical `dataProviderId` validation and admin-time discoverability**
   - **Description:** `IVerticalDefinition.dataProviderId` is a free-text string today (`IVerticalDefinition.ts:16`, `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:125, 156`) with no validation against the registered providers. Add (a) a property-pane Dropdown (instead of free text) populated from `state.registries.dataProviders.getAll().map(p => ({key: p.id, text: p.id}))` so admins pick from the registered list; (b) edit-mode warning in `SpSearchVerticals.tsx` when a vertical references a `dataProviderId` not present in the registry (e.g. typo `'graph'` vs `'graph-search'`), since the orchestrator's silent fallback (`SearchOrchestrator.ts:550-557`) currently masks the misconfiguration; (c) document each shipped provider's `id` in `docs/extensibility-guide.md` ("SharePoint Search provider id: `sharepoint-search` (`SharePointSearchProvider.ts:23`). Graph provider id: `graph-search` (`GraphSearchProvider.ts:109`, configurable via `config.id`). Custom providers must register with a unique id.").
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T3 differentiator. Per-vertical routing is one of the explicit T3 scope items (spec §4.3 T3) and the only one currently with zero validation. A typo today silently routes the People vertical back to SharePoint Search instead of Graph — the People layout still renders rows but they're documents, not personae, with no diagnostic signal.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P1

   - **Source:** spec §4.3 T3 explicit scope item ("per-vertical `dataProviderId` routing"); Phase 6.3 discovery: `SearchOrchestrator.ts:550-557` falls back silently on unknown `dataProviderId`; `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:125, 156` accepts any string from the property pane CollectionData field
   - **Acceptance signal:** Verticals property pane Dropdown for `dataProviderId` lists registered provider ids; typing a non-registered id is impossible (no free text). When a legacy JSON-imported vertical references an unknown id (migration path per `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:114-137`), edit mode shows a warning MessageBar naming the vertical key + the bad id. `docs/extensibility-guide.md` adds the "Built-in provider ids" reference subsection.

   - **Description:** Add a "Multi-Context" tab to `DebugPanel.tsx` (per Phase 4 + T5 plan) that enumerates `window.__sp_search_context_map__` entries: per-context id, urlPrefix, isInitialized flag, registered providers, registered actions, registered layouts, registered filter types, current store snapshot (queryText, vertical, activeFilters count, items.length), and `urlSyncUnsubscribe`-attached/null status. T5.D4's reciprocal note added there.
   - **Source:** Phase 6.3 discovery: `grep -rn '__sp_search_context_map__' src` returns the registry definition (`storeRegistry.ts:36, 44`) and zero consumers — the map is opaque to admins

9. **`disposeStore` regression test and lifecycle smoke harness**
   - **Description:** Add `tests/store/lifecycle.test.ts` covering the full mount/dispose contract introduced in Deliverables 1 and 8: (a) two web parts on context A + two on context B → 4 mounts → map.size === 2; dispose web parts in any order → map.size transitions to 1, then 0; (b) re-mount after full dispose creates fresh contexts (no state, no orchestrator subscription bleed); (c) URL sync popstate listener is added once per context and removed on dispose (assert via `addEventListener` / `removeEventListener` spy); (d) debounce timers are cleared on dispose (assert via `clearTimeout` spy on `urlSyncMiddleware.ts:776-781`); (e) abortController is aborted on dispose (assert against `createStore.ts:78-86` `dispose()` path).
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (b) security and (a) T3 differentiator. Required-Scenario S4 (navigation away/back behavior + store cleanup expectations) needs a regression gate so the work in D1 doesn't decay on the next refactor. Pairs with the Sprint 4 Jest harness fix (CLAUDE.md backlog: "Fix Jest harness `ts-jest`/`jest-util` resolution failure"); this deliverable assumes that fix has landed first.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 1 (the lifecycle wiring under test); Foundations plan Jest harness fix (CLAUDE.md Sprint 4 backlog)
   - **Source:** Required scenario S4; Phase 6.3 discovery: `find tests/store -name '*lifecycle*'` returns 0 hits; existing `disposeStore` (`storeRegistry.ts:245-258`) has no test coverage
   - **Acceptance signal:** `npx jest tests/store/lifecycle.test.ts` passes with five named test cases covering (a)–(e). Each test includes a `__sp_search_context_map__` size assertion and a Spy-based assertion on `removeEventListener` / `clearTimeout` / `AbortController.abort()` invocation count.

10. **Initialization-order diagnostic (close ARCH-003 against T3 surface)**
    - **Description:** ARCH-003 (Still-Open in Appendix A — initialization order dependency not enforced — `storeRegistry.ts:189, 191-198`) lands here because it is most acutely felt in multi-context pages: Context A's Results web part may load before Context A's Filters web part, so the first search runs without `filterConfig` and URL filters silently fail to apply. Add a per-context `_initOrderDiagnostic` to `storeRegistry.ts` that records (a) which web parts have called `initializeSearchContext()`, (b) whether the orchestrator has fired its first `triggerSearch()` yet, (c) whether `filterConfig` was empty at first-search time. In edit mode, surface a warning MessageBar on the Results web part: "First search ran before Filters web part loaded — URL filters may not have been applied. Reload the page to retry." Provide an in-product retry button.
    - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T3 differentiator. The init-order failure mode is invisible today (the comment block at `storeRegistry.ts:191-198` documents the convention but nothing enforces it), and a multi-context page makes it more likely (more web parts, more load races). Closes ARCH-003 against the T3 surface so Foundations doesn't have to re-litigate the multi-context aspect.
    - **Effort:** M
    - **Priority:** P2
    - **Depends on:** Deliverable 2 (consumes the same per-web-part registration registry)
    - **Source:** Appendix A ARCH-003 (Still-Open); Journey B Step 11 [Polish] (URL filters silently lost on slow tenant); Phase 6.3 discovery: `storeRegistry.ts:191-198` documents the convention but provides no programmatic check; Foundations track owns residual ARCH-003 failure modes outside multi-context init order (e.g., single-context Search Box loading before its Verticals)
    - **Acceptance signal:** Load a multi-context page where the Filters web part is artificially delayed (via SPFx render order or DevTools network throttling) — edit mode shows the new MessageBar on the Results web part naming the failure mode; clicking Retry re-runs the search with the now-arrived filterConfig. View mode hides the warning. Unit test in `tests/store/initOrderDiagnostic.test.ts` asserts the diagnostic is set when a search runs before any Filters registration call.

11. **Storybook-style sample page for two-context layout (provisioning + screenshot fixture)**
    - **Description:** Extend `scripts/Provision-TestPages.ps1:319-381` to provision a second multi-context sample (`test-multi-context-tenant-vs-site`) demonstrating the next-most-common scenario (Tenant-wide Knowledge Base context + Site-scoped Documents context). Add `docs/screenshots/multi-context/` with three captures: (a) the rendered page after first paint, (b) the URL bar after typing in both contexts, (c) the DevTools `__sp_search_context_map__` snapshot. Reference these screenshots from D5's documentation page. Updates `docs/provisioning-guide.md` with the new page name and one-line description.
    - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T3 differentiator. D5 is the prose; this is the runnable artefact admins can deploy to their own tenant in 30 seconds and see the moat working. Spec §4.3 T3 explicit scope item ("sample multi-context pages") — current state ships one (`test-multi-context`); a second sample with a different scenario shape stress-tests the documentation against more than one configuration.
    - **Effort:** S
    - **Priority:** P2
    - **Depends on:** Deliverable 5 (docs page consumes the screenshots).
    - **Source:** spec §4.3 T3 explicit scope item ("sample multi-context pages"); Phase 6.3 discovery: `Provision-TestPages.ps1:319-381` ships exactly one multi-context page (`multi-docs` + `multi-people`) with no companion second-shape sample
    - **Acceptance signal:** Running `Provision-TestPages.ps1 -PagesOnly "test-multi-context-tenant-vs-site"` provisions the new page with two distinct contexts. Three PNG fixtures land in `docs/screenshots/multi-context/`. `docs/multi-context-guide.md` (D5) renders both samples side-by-side.

##### Coverage walk (spec §4.3 T3 scope item → mapping)

- **`searchContextId` correctness** → D2 (mismatch warning), D4 (property pane discoverability)
- **URL parameter namespacing (`?ctx1.q=...`)** → D6 (admin-overridable prefix), D3 (alias collision); proven today via `urlSyncMiddleware.ts:79-81` `prefixKey` and `storeRegistry.ts:176, 224-234` re-subscribe path (Current State, BUG-005 Closed in Appendix A)
- **Per-vertical `dataProviderId` routing** → D7 (validation + Dropdown + diagnostic); proven today via `SearchOrchestrator.ts:544-557` (Current State)
- **Cross-context coordination patterns** → Out of Scope item 1 (intentionally absent — isolation is the contract)
- **Sample multi-context pages** → D5 (docs walkthrough), D11 (second sample + screenshots); first sample exists today via `Provision-TestPages.ps1:319-381` (Current State)
- **Isolation guarantees under stress** → D8 (DebugPanel inspection surface), D9 (lifecycle regression tests)
- **Library-component singleton backing (`window.__sp_search_context_map__`)** → proven today via `storeRegistry.ts:36-54` (Current State); D8 surfaces it for admin inspection
- **Regression risks when admins reuse context IDs across pages** → Out of Scope item 4 (cross-page state propagation is by design — same `searchContextId` on a different page legitimately shares state)
- **Required scenario S1 (two contexts on one page)** → Current State proves the substrate (`Provision-TestPages.ps1:319-381`); D4 (discoverability) + D5 (docs) make it self-serve
- **Required scenario S2 (mismatch when isolation expected)** → D2 (mismatch warning)
- **Required scenario S3 (deep-link parameters for two contexts)** → Current State proves the namespace layer (`urlSyncMiddleware.ts:79-81, 776-781`); D3 (alias collision) + D6 (explicit prefix) close the residual gaps
- **Required scenario S4 (navigation away/back + cleanup)** → D1 (refcounted dispose wiring) + D9 (regression tests)

#### Out of scope for v1.0

- **Cross-context publish/subscribe API.** Rationale: Spec §4.3 T3 lists "cross-context coordination patterns" as scope but the architecture intentionally ships isolation as the only contract — adding a coordination API risks turning multi-context pages into a coupled-by-default model that re-creates the PnP Dynamic Data failure mode SP Search exists to avoid. Capture as v2.0 only if user research shows real coordinate-two-contexts demand (e.g. "one search drives a related search").
- **`searchContextId` change live-migration of in-flight state.** Rationale: When the admin changes `searchContextId` from `default` to `hr-search` in property pane, the existing default store keeps its state and a fresh `hr-search` store starts empty. A live-migration would copy state across the boundary atomically. This is rare in practice (admins set the ID once at page-build time, not at runtime) and would re-introduce the cross-context coupling we explicitly reject in Out of Scope item 1. Defer.
- **Per-context CSP nonce and iframe sandbox attribution.** Rationale: SP Search inherits the SharePoint page CSP; per-context security boundaries (e.g. one context can't read another's preview iframe) would require shadow DOM + per-context iframe rewrites. Out of audience-profile scope ("self-serve any tenant") — different product shape. Capture in v2.0 if a multi-tenant or guest-context use case materializes.
- **Cross-page state propagation via tenant-shared backend.** Rationale: Same `searchContextId` on two SharePoint pages currently produces two independent stores (window-backed map is per-tab) — by design, since cross-tab/cross-page sync would require either BroadcastChannel (no SharePoint guarantee) or a tenant-shared list write per state change (perf disaster). Documented as expected behavior in D5; not a deliverable.
- **Telemetry on multi-context usage (how many tenants run two contexts vs one).** Rationale: Out of audience-profile scope at v1.0 (Foundations track owns the broader telemetry decision per spec §4.4); usage telemetry would need to land alongside the tenant-wide opt-in Foundations work, not as a T3-specific gate.
- **Programmatic enforcement of init order (e.g. block `initializeSearchContext` until all expected web parts have registered).** Rationale: ARCH-003 deliverable D10 ships a diagnostic warning instead of a hard enforcement; a hard block would create new failure modes (e.g. a page where the admin removed Filters web part would never finish init). Diagnostic is the correct v1.0 shape; enforcement is post-v1.0 if data shows ongoing init-order pain.
- **Window-key namespace consolidation under a single `window.__sp_search__` object.** The existing `__sp_search_*` prefix is intentionally chosen as the SP Search namespace; forks or unrelated solutions using the same prefix will silently merge. Consolidating the three (and any future) globals — `__sp_search_context_map__`, `__sp_search_init_promises__`, `__sp_search_webpart_registrations__` (introduced by D2) — under one object is deferred to v1.1+ — no observed conflict in the wild and the 1-time migration cost is moderate.

### T4. Admin Experience

#### Current state

T4 is the surface where SP Search proves it is a configurable product, not a custom SI engagement. The substrate is in better shape than the audience profile suggests: nine scenario presets ship, a custom managed-property schema picker exists, edit-mode validation runs on the Results web part, an Admin Dashboard with four panels (Coverage / Quality / Zero-Results / Insights) is wired, and a one-shot provisioning orchestrator covers deploy + lists + page + web parts in a single command. The gaps are concentrated in (a) discoverability of the things admins need first (preset picker buried on page 2; column pickers fall back to free-text), (b) destructive defaults in the provisioning scripts that wipe admin work without confirmation, (c) an Admin Manager toolbox-tile differentiation problem inherited from INC-007, and (d) docs/code drift on preset names and shipped defaults.

The actual T4 surface, by file:

- **Property pane configuration breadth.** Five user-facing web parts plus one inherited admin web part own a combined ~3,034 LOC of `getPropertyPaneConfiguration` + handlers (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:936-1303` 4 pages × 11 groups; `SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:219-459` 4 pages; `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:248-484` 3 pages; `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts:207-389` 2 pages; `SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:194-352` 1 page × 5 groups; `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts:1-21` 21-line subclass).
- **Scenario presets shipped today.** `src/webparts/spSearchResults/presets/searchPresets.ts:64-384` defines **nine** presets: `general`, `documents`, `people`, `news`, `hub-search`, `knowledge-base`, `policy-search`, `account-documents`, `media` — registered in `SCENARIO_PRESETS` at `:423-434`. The PowerShell mirror `scripts/Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1:39-358` defines the same nine with `Invoke-SearchScenarioPage` as the runtime entry point (`:527-706`). `CLAUDE.md` and the spec describe `knowledgeBase` / `hubSearch` / `policySearch` as Sprint 4 backlog — that note is stale; all three are shipped. `account-documents` is shipped in code (`searchPresets.ts:333,433`) and provisioning (`Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1:312`) but missing from `docs/admin-guide.md:108-120` (lists 8 presets + `custom`) and `docs/deployment-guide.md:79-87`.
- **Preset picker UX.** `PropertyPaneChoiceGroup('layoutPreset')` renders inside `MainLayoutsGroupName` on **page 2** of Results (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:1078-1084`); `_buildPresetOptions()` lists 8 (custom + 7 — omits `account-documents`; `people` gated by `_graphOrgService` presence at `:797-800`). `_applyScenarioPreset()` at `:711-746` updates only **Results**-owned properties — `queryTemplate`, layout toggles, selected/compact/grid/sort property collections — and does NOT push the preset's `filterSuggestions` (`searchPresets.ts:92,132,172,208,245,284,324,372,414`) or vertical hints into Filters or Verticals web parts. `:888-890` and `:922-923` revert `layoutPreset` to `'custom'` whenever any layout-related property changes — adding one Card-layout toggle silently demotes the preset.
- **Schema picker.** `src/propertyPaneControls/PropertyPaneSchemaHelper.ts:51-94` wraps a custom `SchemaHelperControl.tsx` panel with a searchable, filterable browser of tenant managed properties (`fetchManagedProperties` + four pivots: All / Refinable / Sortable / Retrievable / Queryable). It is wired to **one field only**: `queryTemplate` on Results (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:965-971`). `selectedPropertiesCollection` (`:976-999`), `compactPropertiesCollection` (`:1129-1145`), `gridPropertiesCollection` (`:1151-1167`), `refinementFiltersCollection.property` (`:1252-1287`), `sortablePropertiesCollection.property` (`:1005-1038`), `SpSearchFiltersWebPart` `filtersCollection.managedProperty`, and `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart` per-vertical `dataProviderId` all fall back to free-text strings.
- **Edit-mode validation.** `validateWebPartConfig` at `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/configValidation.ts:54` produces three-level (`error`/`warning`/`info`) `IConfigWarning[]` rendered as Fluent `MessageBar`s in `SpSearchResults.tsx:722-750`. Today validates: default-layout-not-enabled, grid-with-no-columns, layout-toggles-versus-availableLayouts mismatch, queryTemplate token presence. Does NOT validate: managed property names exist in tenant schema (typo `LastModifedTime` ships silently empty); `searchContextId` connectivity to other web parts on the page (T3.D2 owns); `refinementFiltersCollection` operator/value pairs; `collapseSpecification` field is Sortable (CLAUDE.md Data Rule #2 fails silently); `expectedSiteUrls` URLs are reachable. Filters / Verticals / Manager have **zero** equivalent edit-mode validation surface.
- **Admin Dashboard depth.** `AdminDashboard.tsx:1-281` is a 4-section accordion: `CoverageStatsSection` (`:194-213`, 149-line component), `QualityMetricsSection` (`:215-234`, 108 lines), `ZeroResultsPanel` (`:236-254`, 249 lines), `SearchInsightsPanel` (`:256-275`, 559 lines). Time-range pivot (30/60/90 days at `:26-30`) refresh-all button at `:186-190`. Ships behind a property pane toggle `enableDashboard` (`SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:232-234`). Admin Manager manifest defaults to `enableDashboard: true` (`SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.manifest.json:26`); legacy Manager manifest does not include the field. Routing in `SpSearchManager.tsx:139-302` gates Coverage/Health/Insights/Dashboard tabs by individual property toggles.
- **Provisioning script robustness.** `Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` (557 lines) Phase 4 at `:373-377` unconditionally calls `Get-PnPPage` then `Remove-PnPPage -Identity $PageName -Force` if a page matching `-PageName` (default `"Search"` at `:33`) exists — no `-WhatIf`, no `[CmdletBinding(SupportsShouldProcess)]`, no confirm prompt, no `-Force` opt-in. `:488` writes `coverageProfilesCollection` from `Get-SeededCoverageProfiles` (`:76-100`) which returns 10 hardcoded document libraries (`:50-61`) + 10 hardcoded custom lists (`:63-74`); the Admin Dashboard's Coverage tab opens broken on day 1 of any tenant that hasn't run `Provision-TestData.ps1`. `:42-48` defines web part lookup names — `WP_SEARCH_FILTERS = "SPSearchFilters"` and `WP_SEARCH_VERTICALS = "SPSearchVerticals"` differ from the manifest titles `"SP Search Filters"` / `"SP Search Verticals"`, risking silent blank web part insertion per MEMORY.md PnP-3.x notes (overlaps Foundations). `Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1:629-657` writes `filterCollection` and `verticalCollection` (singular) where the manifests expect `filtersCollection` / `verticalsCollection` (plural) — silent fallback to manifest defaults.
- **Default value sanity for unknown tenants.** Manager manifest ships `enableSavedSearches=false`, `enableSharedSearches=false`, `enableCollections=false`, `enableHistory=false` (`SpSearchManagerWebPart.manifest.json:30-33`); Admin Manager ships the same plus `enableDashboard=true` (`SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.manifest.json:24-29`). `docs/admin-guide.md:221-226` claims all four user-facing toggles default to `true` — direct docs/code drift surfaced as Journey A Step 10 [Confusion] (Foundations owns the doc fix; T4 owns whether the shipped defaults are right for first-time tenants). `solution.developer.mpnId = "Undefined-1.21.1"` (`config/package-solution.json:15`) is a generator default visible in the SharePoint admin "Apps you can add" pane.
- **Admin Manager differentiation.** Two admin-manager web parts ship in the same package: `SpSearchManagerWebPart` titled "SP Search Manager (Legacy)" (`SpSearchManagerWebPart.manifest.json:21-22`) and `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` titled "SP Search Admin Manager" (`SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.manifest.json:14-15`), both icon `SearchAndApps`, both `Advanced` group. `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts:1-21` is a 21-line subclass that adds only a `DebugCollector.registerWebPart` call to `onInit`. INC-007 in Appendix A is Changed-Form — manifest defaults differ but behavior is 100% inherited.
- **Property pane error handling.** Three of six web parts implement `onGetErrorMessage` on the `searchContextId` field (`SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:367-377`, `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:1217-1222`, `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:454-462`); Verticals, Manager, and Admin Manager do not. Box also validates `newPageUrl` for the BUG-004 XSS guard (`:270-279`). No other property pane field has an `onGetErrorMessage`. PnP `PropertyFieldCollectionData` cells (selected/compact/grid/sort/refinement/coverage-profiles/filters/verticals/scopes) accept any free-text string with no per-cell validation hook beyond the field-level `required` flag.

Closed/Changed-Form items already in the T4 surface (per Appendix A): BUG-001 (`operatorBetweenFilters` watched), BUG-002 (`queryInputTransformation` watched), MISS-008 (search scope configuration UI). Still-Open items in T4's path: MISS-001 (`queryInputTransformation` end-to-end pipeline incomplete — surfaced in property pane but not fully applied), MISS-002 (`operatorBetweenFilters` filter execution path may not consistently apply OR semantics), INC-007 Changed-Form (Admin Manager 100% inherited from Manager — only manifest defaults + DebugCollector hook differ).

#### Gap to "amazing"

The audience profile is "any SPFx-capable tenant, self-serve, no SI hand-holding" — and T4 is the surface where the admin decides in the first 30 minutes whether SP Search is a configurable product or a custom build. Today the gap is concentrated in five places, each independently shippable. **First, the provisioning scripts are unsafe by default**: `Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` silently destroys any page named `Search` on every re-run with no `-WhatIf`, no confirm prompt, no `-Force` opt-in — the admin who tweaks the auto-provisioned page in the SharePoint UI and then re-runs the script (because they want to add a second context, or fix a typo, or roll back a partial install) loses everything. Pair that with seeded coverage profiles that point at hardcoded test-data URLs (`CorporatePolicies`, `SalesMaterials`, …) that don't exist on a clean tenant, and the very first thing the admin sees post-publish is the Admin Dashboard rendering broken stat cards. **Second, the preset picker is buried and stops at the Results web part boundary**: nine presets ship (correcting the stale "Sprint 4 backlog" note in CLAUDE.md), but the `PropertyPaneChoiceGroup` lives on page 2 of the Results pane inside the layouts group, the picker omits `account-documents` entirely, and selecting `documents` does not push the preset's `filterSuggestions` or vertical hints into the Filters / Verticals web parts — so the admin who picks a preset still has to hand-key the filter and vertical setup that the preset was supposed to deliver. The "preset" promise is half-kept. **Third, the schema picker is wired to one field**: `PropertyPaneSchemaHelper` is a real product surface that browses tenant managed properties with refinable/sortable/retrievable/queryable filters — but it only assists `queryTemplate`. Every column picker, every filter `managedProperty` field, every sort property, every collapse spec, and every per-vertical `dataProviderId` falls back to free-text. A typo in `LastModifedTime` produces a silently empty column at runtime with no diagnostic anywhere. **Fourth, the Admin Dashboard's first paint is fragile**: the four panels are wired and look polished when populated, but Coverage opens to broken cards on day 1, Quality / Insights have no per-user or per-vertical breakdown (UX-006 Still-Open), the zero-results panel needs manual refresh (UX-005 Changed-Form), and CTR is a single window-wide number with no week-over-week trend (UX-007 Still-Open). The dashboard feels like four monitors taped to a wall instead of a curated admin surface. **Fifth, Admin Manager differentiation is missing**: two manifests ship two near-identical toolbox tiles, both titled "Manager", both icon `SearchAndApps`, one labelled `(Legacy)` — and the only behavioral difference is one `DebugCollector` call. INC-007 closure left the architectural gap intact. The architecture is mostly right; what is missing is the polish that turns "configurable" into "configurable in 15 minutes by an admin who has never seen this product."

#### Deliverables

1. **Provisioning script safety: `-WhatIf` / confirm-on-destructive-default across the four destructive provisioning scripts**
   - **Description:** SupportsShouldProcess retrofit on the four scripts that today perform unconditional destructive operations: (1) `Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` Phase 4 page-removal block (`:373-377`); (2) `Provision-SPSearchLists.ps1` unconditional list re-creation paths (any `Remove-PnPList` / `Add-PnPList -Force` chain that overwrites an existing list with admin-customised columns/views); (3) `Map-CrawledProperties.ps1` schema rewrites (any `Set-PnPSearchConfiguration` overwrite path that wipes existing tenant mappings); (4) `Provision-TestData.ps1` content seeding (any `Remove-*` / re-seed loop that wipes admin content created post-seed). Each script gets `[CmdletBinding(SupportsShouldProcess = $true, ConfirmImpact = 'High')]` (the pattern already used by `Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1:528`); each destructive call wrapped in `if ($PSCmdlet.ShouldProcess($Target, 'Operation'))` so admins get Y/N prompt by default and can pre-approve via `-Confirm:$false`. Each script also gains a `-Force` switch as the explicit opt-in path; without `-Force` AND without a confirm-yes, abort with clear copy ("Item 'X' already exists. Re-run with -Force to overwrite, or pick a different -Name"). Per-path `-WhatIf` testing: every wrapped destructive call must produce a "What if: …" line and exit cleanly without executing. Document new behavior in `docs/deployment-guide.md` and add header-comment one-liner in each script. Effort reflects four scripts × multiple destructive paths × per-path `-WhatIf` test coverage.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (e) Journey A Step 4 [Blocker] (admin has no documented workaround — `Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` silently destroys page customizations on every re-run) and (d) "would prevent install" — second-run is the most common admin scenario (typo recovery, scope refinement, partial-failure retry), and a tool that destroys work on the operation an admin runs second is uninstallable in practice. The same shape repeats on the other three scripts: `Provision-SPSearchLists.ps1` will overwrite hidden lists that admins extended with custom columns; `Map-CrawledProperties.ps1` will wipe tenant managed-property mappings made out-of-band; `Provision-TestData.ps1` will re-seed over admin-created content.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** none
   - **Source:** Journey A Step 4 [Blocker]; Phase 6.4 discovery: `grep -n 'SupportsShouldProcess\|ShouldProcess' scripts/*.ps1` returns one hit (`Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1:528`) across 10 scripts
   - **Acceptance signal:** Running `.\Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1 -SiteUrl ... -ClientId ...` a second time on a tenant with an existing `Search` page prompts for Y/N before removal; passing `-WhatIf` reports "What if: Performing the operation 'Remove existing page' on target 'Search'." without executing; passing `-Force` re-executes without prompting; absence of both prompts and exits with non-zero. Same shape proven on `Provision-SPSearchLists.ps1` (re-running after a list edit prompts before overwrite), `Map-CrawledProperties.ps1` (re-running after a manual mapping prompts before rewrite), `Provision-TestData.ps1` (re-running after admin content additions prompts before re-seed). PSScriptAnalyzer rule `PSShouldProcess` reports zero violations on all four scripts.

2. **Scenario preset picker promotion + completeness**
   - **Description:** Two fixes that share the same Results-web-part property-pane refactor. (a) **Move the picker to page 1 group 1**: relocate `PropertyPaneChoiceGroup('layoutPreset', ...)` from `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:1078-1084` (page 2 inside `MainLayoutsGroupName`) to a new top-of-page 1 `ScenarioGroupName` group above the existing `DataGroupName`. (b) **Complete preset coverage in `_buildPresetOptions()`** (`:784-803`) **plus people-gate refactor with graceful degradation**: add `account-documents` to the options array (currently omitted despite shipping in `searchPresets.ts:333,433` and `Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1:312`); keep the `people` preset selectable when Graph Org Service is unconfigured (the preset's curated People-layout column set ships independent of Graph) but render a property-pane Fluent `MessageBar` warning when `people` is selected without `_graphOrgService`: "People preset selected but Graph Org Service is not configured — presence and org-chart fields will be empty." Verify no hard crash in People-layout cell renderers when presence/orgchart props are null (read `src/webparts/spSearchResults/cellRenderers/PersonaCellRenderer.tsx` and any sibling People-layout renderers before removing the existing `_graphOrgService` gate at `:797-800`). If any cell renderer hard-crashes on null presence/orgchart input, fix the renderer FIRST (null-coalesce + fallback render path) OR keep the gate and ship D2(b) as warning-only with the gate intact — pick whichever is smaller. Bundle (a) + (b) is a single PR because both touch `_buildPresetOptions` + the page-1 reorganisation in the same property-pane refactor.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator (presets are a Better-than-PnP item per Appendix C "Scenario presets" — only if admins can find and complete them) and (e) Journey A Step 8 [Confusion] (preset picker on page 2 — admins who never reach page 2 miss the curated starter). The 9-shipped vs 8-listed discrepancy compounds: the picker's omission of `account-documents` plus the doc list's omission of `account-documents` (`docs/admin-guide.md:108-120`) means the preset effectively does not exist for self-serve admins. The people-gate change converts a silent omission ("People disappeared from the picker — is it broken?") into an explicit graceful-degradation warning admins can act on.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** none
   - **Source:** Journey A Step 8 [Confusion] (preset picker buried on page 2); Phase 6.4 discovery: `_buildPresetOptions()` at `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:784-803` lists 8 of 9 shipped presets and gates `people` on `_graphOrgService`
   - **Acceptance signal:** Open Results property pane — page 1 group 1 is "Scenario" with the preset ChoiceGroup as its first field. The picker lists all 9 options (Custom + General + Documents + Hub Search + Knowledge Base + Policy Search + News + Media + People + Account Documents) regardless of Graph Org Service state. Selecting `people` on a tenant without Graph Org Service configured renders a yellow MessageBar: "People preset selected but Graph Org Service is not configured — presence and org-chart fields will be empty." People-layout view-mode render does not crash on null presence/orgchart values.

3. **Wire `PropertyPaneSchemaHelper` to all managed-property fields**
   - **Description:** Replace the free-text managed-property cells with `PropertyPaneSchemaHelper` (or an in-cell variant of the same `SchemaHelperControl`) across every web part property pane field that today accepts a managed property as a string. Concretely: `selectedPropertiesCollection.property` (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:984-996`) — currently `placeholder: 'LastModifiedTime'` free-text; `compactPropertiesCollection.property` (`:1129-1145`); `gridPropertiesCollection.property` (`:1151-1167`); `sortablePropertiesCollection.property` (`:1012-1019`); `refinementFiltersCollection.property` (`:1259-1266`); `collapseSpecification` (`:1288-1291`) — pre-validate against `sortable === true` per CLAUDE.md Data Rule #2; `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts:259-415` `filtersCollection.managedProperty`. For `PropertyFieldCollectionData` cells where SchemaHelper cannot be embedded directly (PnP control limitation), add a "Browse Schema" link in the field description that opens the same panel and writes the chosen value back via `changeCallback`. Cache the schema fetch (`fetchManagedProperties`) once per property-pane lifecycle to avoid N calls when admin opens N collection rows.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator and (c) data integrity. A typo in `LastModifedTime` ships a silently empty column at runtime with no diagnostic — admins never connect "my Date Modified column is blank" to "I misspelled the managed property in the property pane three days ago." The schema picker is built and proven for `queryTemplate`; extending it across the full surface is a finite refactor.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** none
   - **Source:** Journey A Step 8 [Confusion] (schema validation absent on column / filter / sort pickers); Phase 6.4 discovery: `grep -rn 'PropertyPaneSchemaHelper' src/webparts` returns one consumer (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:965`) for `queryTemplate` only despite ~10 other managed-property fields across the property panes
   - **Acceptance signal:** Opening Results property pane → page 1 → "Selected Properties" collection — each row's `property` cell offers a schema browser link that filters by `retrievable`. Typing a non-existent property in the cell shows a per-cell error before save (e.g. "`LastModifedTime` is not a managed property in this tenant — did you mean `LastModifiedTime`?"). `collapseSpecification` field rejects non-sortable properties before save with explicit copy. Manual: configure a fresh Results web part with all columns picked from the browser; reload — every column renders. Unit test in `tests/propertyPaneControls/schemaHelper.test.ts` covers the existence + sortable-required validation paths.

4. **Coverage Profile sane defaults: tenant-aware seeding instead of hardcoded test-data URLs**
   - **Description:** Refactor `Get-SeededCoverageProfiles` (`Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1:76-100`) to default to **tenant-discovered** sources instead of hardcoded test-data names (`PROVISIONED_DOCUMENT_LIBRARIES` at `:50-61`, `PROVISIONED_CUSTOM_LISTS` at `:63-74`). Implementation: enumerate the target site's actual document libraries via `Get-PnPList -Includes BaseTemplate | Where-Object { $_.BaseTemplate -eq 101 -and -not $_.Hidden }`, take the top N (configurable via `-MaxSeededLibraries`, default 5), and write coverage profiles that point at real list URLs. If `-UseTestData` is explicitly passed, fall back to today's hardcoded set. In parallel, change the `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.manifest.json:24-29` default `coverageProfilesCollection: []` so an admin who adds the Admin Manager to a page **without** running the provisioning script sees a clear empty-state ("Configure coverage profiles in the property pane to begin monitoring") instead of broken stat cards — the empty-state already exists in `CoverageStatsSection.tsx:48-50` but is hidden behind the seeded-profile-points-at-nonexistent-URL failure path. Document tenant-aware defaults in `docs/admin-guide.md` Coverage Profile section.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator and (e) Journey A Step 11 [Polish] (the Admin Dashboard's Coverage tab is the first impression the admin or end user sees post-publish — broken stats are the worst possible first impression). Pairs with D1's destructive-default fix; both are install-time-blockers caused by aggressive scripted defaults that assume the test-data tenant.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 1 (both ship as part of the `Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` safety/sanity refactor)
   - **Source:** Journey A Step 4 [Confusion] (seeded coverage profiles point at non-existent test-data URLs); Journey A Step 11 [Polish] (broken stats are the first thing the admin sees post-publish)
   - **Acceptance signal:** Running `.\Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` on a clean tenant without `Provision-TestData.ps1` having been run first: the resulting Admin Dashboard Coverage tab renders real itemCount / freshness data from the actual top-5 site libraries, not broken cards. Adding the Admin Manager web part to a page without running any provisioning script renders the Coverage panel's "Configure coverage profiles" empty state with a CTA link to the property pane. `-UseTestData` switch restores the previous behavior for the test tenant.

5. **Edit-mode validation expansion: cross-web-part + collection-cell + connectivity warnings**
   - **Description:** Extend the `validateWebPartConfig` pattern (`src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/configValidation.ts:54`) into a shared `src/libraries/spSearchStore/configValidation/` module consumable by all six web parts. Add validators: (a) `validateManagedPropertyCollection(collection, schema)` — flags free-text values not present in the cached schema fetch, with per-row error messages rendered as Fluent `MessageBar`s in edit mode; (b) `validateRefinementFilterCollection(collection)` — flags missing operators, value/operator type mismatches (e.g. `range` operator with non-range value), and unsupported operators per `SearchService.buildRefinementFilters`; (c) `validateCoverageProfileSourceUrls(profiles, currentSite)` — flags URLs that don't begin with `/sites/`, `/teams/`, or `https://<tenant>.sharepoint.com/`; (d) `validateExpectedSiteUrls(urls)` — `SpSearchManagerWebPart.ts:255-260` field accepts free-text multi-line; flag malformed URLs and sites not reachable via Graph (best-effort, no blocking). **Ownership of the `dataProviderId` validator (T3.D7 ↔ T4.D5):** T3.D7 ships the canonical `dataProviderId` validator at `src/libraries/spSearchStore/configValidation/dataProviderId.ts`; T4.D5 consumes it from the Verticals web part property pane and surfaces it via shared validation infra alongside the Filters / Manager / Admin Manager validators introduced here — no duplicate implementation. Surface validators on Filters (`SpSearchFiltersWebPart` config), Verticals (consumes T3.D7's validator), Manager (coverage profiles), and Admin Manager (expected sites). Each web part renders results in an edit-mode-only MessageBar block at component root, mirroring `SpSearchResults.tsx:722-750`.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator and (c) data integrity. The Results web part already shows admins what good looks like — extending the same pattern across the surface costs less than the bugs it prevents (silently empty columns, malformed coverage profiles, unreachable expected sites, refinement filters that never execute).
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 3 (schema fetch caching is the substrate the managed-property validator consumes); T3.D7 (per-vertical `dataProviderId` validation — coordinate so the Verticals validator surface is single, not double-implemented). T3.D7's reciprocal note added there.
   - **Source:** Journey A Step 8 [Confusion] (no schema validation); Journey A Step 10 [Confusion] (item-level permission has no in-product confirmation); Phase 6.4 discovery: `grep -rn 'validateWebPartConfig\|validate.*Config' src/webparts` returns matches only in `spSearchResults` — no equivalent on the other 5 web parts
   - **Acceptance signal:** Configure Filters web part with a `managedProperty` typo `Authoer` — edit-mode MessageBar lists the typo with Did-You-Mean alternative. Configure Manager Coverage Profile with a malformed `https://` URL — MessageBar lists the row. Configure Admin Manager `expectedSiteUrls` with a non-tenant URL — warning displayed. Admin clicking the warning gets focus into the offending property pane field. Unit tests in `tests/configValidation/*.test.ts` cover all four validators with positive + negative cases.

6. **Admin Manager differentiation — fork (Path B) to close INC-007 against T4**
   - **Description:** INC-007 (Changed-Form in Appendix A) shipped manifest defaults that disable user-facing tabs but the behavior is 100% inherited (`SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts:1-21` adds only `DebugCollector.registerWebPart`). v1.0 ships **Path B (fork)**: keep both web parts, make `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` a real subclass — add an admin-only property pane page (Coverage Profiles + Expected Sites + Time Range Defaults + ManageWeb-required gate), suppress all user-facing toggles from the property pane (`enableSavedSearches` etc. should not appear in Admin Manager's pane at all), ship a distinct icon (`Diagnostic` or `BIDashboard` in place of `SearchAndApps`), and rename the SpSearchManager manifest to drop the misleading "(Legacy)" copy. Telemetry destination URL field (admin-only property pane group) writes to Foundations D9's `SearchTelemetryConfig` SP list — surfaces the `DestinationEndpoint` value the transport service consumes; cross-track with Foundations.D9 (without this surface or T4.D9's Pre-Flight tab equivalent, the list is admin-edit-only at v1.0). Path B chosen over Path A because Path A (fold both into one web part with a `mode: 'user' | 'admin'` ChoiceGroup) carries non-trivial SPFx upgrade risk: any tenant page with existing `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` instances loses those instances on package upgrade when the web-part manifest disappears, and that requires manifest-redirect or alias plumbing which has not been validated for SP Search's solution-version + tenant-app-catalog upgrade flow. **Path A explicitly out of scope for v1.0** — folded into Out of scope below as a v1.1+ candidate pending an SPFx migration story for tenants with existing `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` instances on pages.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator and (e) Journey A Step 6 [Confusion] (two near-identical "Manager" tiles in the toolbox with no other differentiation, no documented workaround). The "(Legacy)" copy actively misleads — it implies SpSearchManagerWebPart is deprecated when in fact every Admin Manager call still goes through it via inheritance. This is the most concrete in-product lie in the audit. Path B closes the lookalike issue and removes the "(Legacy)" copy without breaking existing tenant pages.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** none. T5.D8 takes a downstream cross-track dep — Admin Manager fork is the natural home for the telemetry opt-in property pane group; coordinate sequencing in Sprint 5.
   - **Source:** Appendix A INC-007 (Changed-Form); Journey A Step 6 [Confusion]
   - **Acceptance signal:** SPFx toolbox shows two "SP Search Manager" tiles with distinct icons + distinct property pane shapes (User-facing Manager: SearchAndApps icon, user-tab toggles only; Admin Manager: Diagnostic/BIDashboard icon, admin-only property page with Coverage Profiles + Expected Sites). `grep -rn 'Legacy' src/webparts/spSearchManager` returns 0 hits. Existing tenant pages with `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` instances continue to render after package upgrade. INC-007 row in Appendix A flips Closed in the next audit cycle.

9. **Admin pre-flight check: tenant-readiness panel in Admin Manager**
   - **Description:** Add a "Pre-Flight" tab to the Admin Manager (gated by `enableHealth` or a new `enablePreflight` toggle) that runs an admin-time tenant-readiness scan and surfaces a green/yellow/red status grid. Checks: (a) `webApiPermissionRequests` declared in `config/package-solution.json` (Journey A Step 1 [Polish] — `People.Read` for Graph people search currently absent); (b) hidden lists exist with correct schema (`SearchSavedQueries`, `SearchHistory`, `SearchCollections`, including the `IsZeroResult` Boolean field on `SearchHistory` per CLAUDE.md Data Rule #7); (c) `SearchHistory` has `ReadSecurity=2 WriteSecurity=2` per `Provision-SPSearchLists.ps1:230-234` (Journey A Step 10 [Confusion]); (d) tenant managed-property mappings exist for the columns referenced by the active scenario preset (consumes D3's schema fetch); (e) tenant has at least one search content source (`Get-PnPSearchSettings` equivalent via REST). Each row links to the doc / script / property pane that fixes it. Output: a single screenshot the admin can give a peer or attach to a support ticket — the support-bundle parallel for T5.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator and (d) "would prevent install". The tenant-readiness gates today are spread across 8 different docs / scripts / property pane surfaces; an admin landing on a clean tenant cannot tell whether their install is "missing one mapping" or "fundamentally broken." A single in-product readiness scan is the difference between a 30-minute install and a 4-hour debug session.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 2 (preset coverage — pre-flight surfaces preset selection vs. shipped-presets gap), Deliverable 4 (Coverage Profile defaults — pre-flight runs against real tenant lists, not test-data), Deliverable 3 (schema fetch is the substrate), Deliverable 5 (consumes the shared validator surface so pre-flight rows reuse validation copy and field-focus links), Foundations docs sweep (deferred — pre-flight "Fix this" links land on stable doc anchors)
   - **Source:** Journey A Step 9 [Confusion] (re-index dependency invisible); Journey A Step 10 [Confusion] (item-level permission unverifiable in-product); Phase 6.4 discovery: `grep -rn 'webApiPermissionRequests' config` returns 0 hits despite `docs/admin-guide.md:240-242` documenting `People.Read` requirement
   - **Acceptance signal:** Pre-Flight tab in Admin Manager renders a 5-row checklist with green/yellow/red icons and per-row "Fix this" links. Running on a fresh tenant before any provisioning shows 4-of-5 red with actionable copy and links. After running `Setup-SPSearchSite.ps1` + `Map-CrawledProperties.ps1`, all 5 rows go green. Single screenshot of the tab is sufficient evidence of tenant readiness for a peer hand-off.

Passing `-ReleaseArtifactUrl 'https://github.com/.../v1.0.0/sp-search.sppkg'` downloads the GitHub Releases artifact and deploys it without a local build.

12. **Cross-web-part scenario preset propagation via `recordPresetSuggestion` + Filters/Verticals listeners**
    - **Description:** Split out from D2(c) because it touches multiple web parts plus a new store-registry API, and isn't credibly a single-PR change with the page-1 reorganisation. Extend `_applyScenarioPreset()` (`SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:711-746`) to also write `filtersCollection` (mapped from `preset.filterSuggestions` at `searchPresets.ts:92,132,172,208,245,284,324,372,414`) and `verticalsCollection` hints to the store via a new `recordPresetSuggestion(searchContextId, preset)` API on `storeRegistry.ts`. Filters and Verticals web parts subscribe in edit mode and render a Fluent `MessageBar` "The Documents preset suggests four filters and three verticals — apply now?" with a one-click button that overwrites their respective collection properties. View mode unaffected. Implementation surfaces: (1) new `recordPresetSuggestion` / `consumePresetSuggestion` API on `storeRegistry.ts` (parallel to the existing `recordWebPartContextId` pattern); (2) edit-mode subscription wiring on Filters web part component; (3) edit-mode subscription wiring on Verticals web part component; (4) cross-web-part propagation tests (admin selects preset on Results → MessageBar appears on Filters within current property-pane session).
    - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T4 differentiator (presets only deliver value if they propagate beyond the Results web part — picking `documents` should not require admins to hand-key the corresponding filter and vertical setup) and (e) Journey A Step 8 [Confusion] (preset only updates Results — Filters/Verticals must be hand-keyed). D2 ships the picker correctness; D12 ships the propagation that makes the picker useful end-to-end.
    - **Effort:** M
    - **Priority:** P1
    - **Depends on:** Deliverable 2 (D2 ships the corrected picker that produces the preset-applied event D12 listens for)
    - **Source:** Journey A Step 8 [Confusion] (preset does not propagate); Phase 6.4 discovery: `_applyScenarioPreset()` at `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:711-746` only updates Results-owned properties, ignoring `preset.filterSuggestions` and vertical hints
    - **Acceptance signal:** Selecting `documents` in the Results property pane in edit mode renders an in-page MessageBar on the Filters web part offering to apply the four `documents` filterSuggestions; clicking "Apply" populates `filtersCollection` and the Filters web part re-renders with the suggested four filters. Same offer appears on Verticals. View mode shows no MessageBar. Re-selecting the same preset within the same edit-mode session does not duplicate the MessageBar.

##### Coverage walk (spec §4.3 T4 scope item → mapping)

- **Property pane discoverability** → D2 (preset picker page 1 + completeness), D12 (cross-web-part propagation), D11 (help link surface); proven today via `SpSearchResultsWebPart.ts:1078` (currently buried)
- **Scenario presets (`general`/`documents`/`news`/`people`/`media` + `knowledgeBase`/`hubSearch`/`policySearch` + `account-documents`)** → Current State proves all 9 ship today via `searchPresets.ts:64-384` (first preset id to last; plus `custom` as the unset state, totaling 10 ChoiceGroup options); D2 fixes picker-omits-`account-documents` + people-gate graceful degradation; D12 ships cross-web-part propagation; spec §4.3 wording "pending" is stale — corrected in Current State. Note: CLAUDE.md and MEMORY.md inherit the same stale "Sprint 4 backlog" note for these three; doc updates are owned by Foundations (stale-docs deliverable)
- **Schema picker UX** → D3 (extend `PropertyPaneSchemaHelper` to all managed-property fields); proven today via `PropertyPaneSchemaHelper.ts:51-94` for `queryTemplate` only
- **Edit-mode validation/lint** → D5 (cross-web-part validators); current state proves the pattern via `configValidation.ts:54` for Results only
- **Provisioning script robustness** → D1 (`-WhatIf` / confirm across all four destructive scripts), D4 (Coverage Profile sane defaults); spec items overlap with Foundations (gulp-vs-heft script breakage owned there)
- **Admin Dashboard depth (Coverage / Quality / Health / Insights)** → D7 (UX-005/006/007 closure + first-paint sanity), D9 (pre-flight tab); Current State proves all four panels ship today via `AdminDashboard.tsx:1-281`
- **Property pane error handling** → D8 (parity across all six web parts); Current State proves three of six have any `onGetErrorMessage` today
- **Default value sanity for unknown tenants** → D4 (Coverage Profile defaults), D10 (mpnId + tenant catalog), D9 (pre-flight check surfaces tenant-readiness gaps); Current State logs the docs-vs-shipped-defaults drift on Manager toggles (Foundations owns the doc fix)
- **Admin Manager differentiation (INC-007 Changed-Form)** → D6 (Path B fork; Path A fold deferred to v1.1+); Current State proves the 100%-inherited subclass at `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts:1-21`

##### Appendix A items intersecting T4 (not in spec §4.3 scope mapping)

- **MISS-001 (`queryInputTransformation` end-to-end)** → Out of Scope item 1 (Sprint 4 backlog from CLAUDE.md, separately tracked); D5 surfaces a stopgap "transformation set but pipeline incomplete" warning until ship.
- **MISS-002 (`operatorBetweenFilters` filter execution)** → Out of Scope item 2 (Sprint 4 backlog); D5 surfaces a stopgap "OR semantics may not apply consistently across filter groups" warning until ship.

##### Effort total

**12 deliverables (4 P0 / 6 P1 / 2 P2)**: P0 = D1 (L) + D2 (M) + D3 (L) + D4 (M); P1 = D5 (L) + D6 (L) + D7 (L) + D8 (M) + D9 (L) + D12 (M); P2 = D10 (S) + D11 (M). Effort tier midpoints (S ≤ 4h ≈ 0.5d; M = ½–1d, midpoint 0.75d; L = 1–3d, midpoint 2d; XL > 3d, midpoint 4d): **6 × L (12d) + 5 × M (3.75d) + 1 × S (0.5d) ≈ 16 dev-days midpoint**, honest range **12–26 dev-days** depending on which sub-item bundles ship as separate PRs vs. unified refactors and how much per-script `-WhatIf` test coverage D1 absorbs. (Earlier total of "18–28" overstated because D1 was scoped to one script as M when the description called out four scripts, and D2 was an L bundle that absorbed cross-web-part propagation work without sizing the additional store-registry API surface; D12 carries that work explicitly now.)

#### Out of scope for v1.0

- **Folding Admin Manager into Manager via `mode` ChoiceGroup (D6 Path A).** Rationale: deletes the `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` manifest and exposes a `mode: 'user' | 'admin'` toggle on a unified Manager. Defers to v1.1+ pending an SPFx migration story for tenants with existing `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart` instances on pages — without manifest-redirect or alias plumbing validated for SP Search's solution-version + tenant-app-catalog upgrade flow, package upgrade silently breaks any page that already hosts the admin web part. D6 ships **Path B (fork)** in v1.0 instead; revisit Path A once an SPFx upgrade story exists or ample tenant data shows no installed Admin Manager instances in the wild.
- **D2's third sub-item — cross-web-part scenario preset propagation as a single-PR bundle.** Originally bundled into D2; split into D12 because it touches Filters + Verticals web parts plus a new `recordPresetSuggestion` API on `storeRegistry.ts` and isn't credibly a single-PR change with the page-1 reorganisation. Not deferred — D12 is in scope for v1.0 — only the bundling claim is rejected.
- **`queryInputTransformation` full end-to-end pipeline (MISS-001).** Rationale: BUG-002 closure (orchestrator now watches the property) addresses the immediate symptom; the broader transformation pipeline is Sprint 4 backlog per `CLAUDE.md` and is one specific T4 scope item. Surfacing the property without full pipeline runs the risk of admins setting transformations that silently no-op; D5's edit-mode validation can flag "transformation set but pipeline incomplete" as a stopgap warning until MISS-001 ships in Sprint 4. Not slotting into v1.0.
