The Foundations D2 smoke checklist includes type-check as a pre-merge step.

4. **HTML sanitizer adoption + `window.location.href` security review**
   - **Description:** Two security-hardening sub-items grouped because both are "sweep + adopt" shape rather than implement-new and both consume the same security-review attention budget: (a) **Adopt `spfx-toolkit/lib/utilities/htmlUtils/sanitizeHtml`** (Appendix B HTML sanitization Adopt) — replace the local `sanitizeSummaryHtml` (`src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/documentTitleUtils.ts:158`) used at `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/ListLayout.tsx:69` `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`. Toolkit sanitizer ships explicit `ALLOWED_TAGS` + `LINK_ATTRIBUTES` allowlists and `isSafeUrl` predicate; centralizes the policy and reduces XSS surface. Remove the local implementation (`documentTitleUtils.ts:155-end`) once the call site migrates. Verify by re-running the BUG-004 closure smoke (`Author:&lt;script&gt;` summary string) renders escaped, not executed. (b) **Sweep the 7 `window.location.href` sites** — each of `src/libraries/spSearchStore/providers/QuickResultsSuggestionProvider.ts:80`, `src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/SpSearchManager.tsx:369,548,644,646`, `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/SpSearchResults.tsx:568,570` against the BUG-004 hardening pattern (validate target before navigation; reject `javascript:`, `data:`, etc.). The Box site `:358` is already hardened. Add a centralized `src/libraries/spSearchStore/utils/safeNavigate.ts` helper exporting `safeNavigate(target: string): boolean` that all 8 sites consume — single policy, single enforcement point. ESLint custom rule (or comment-based pattern marker) flags any new `window.location.href = X` write that does not flow through `safeNavigate`. Bundle is justified because both (a) and (b) ship in the same PR-shaped security-review pass against the in-product navigation/render surface; splitting them into two PRs duplicates the reviewer attention without adding value. Pairs with T5.D6 (PII redaction at the logging layer is the privacy half of the same security-review attention budget; coordinate sequencing in Sprint 4).
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (b) security. BUG-004 closure (Closed in Appendix A) hardened ONE of the 8 navigation sites; the other 7 inherit the same risk shape (any string assigned to `window.location.href` can be `javascript:alert(1)` if the source is an untrusted property). HTML sanitizer adoption reduces XSS surface centrally rather than maintaining the local implementation. Pairs with T2.D3 (saved-search JSON schema validation, SEC-004 Still-Open) — T2.D3 closes the input side, this deliverable closes the output / navigation side. P1 (not P0) because no new exposure has been demonstrated in the 7 unhardened sites (the property values are admin-configured, not user-typed); the hardening is precautionary.
   - **Effort:** M
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** none. T2.D3 covers the parallel JSON schema validation at the input side; coordinate so both ship in Sprint 4 alongside this output-side hardening.
   - **Source:** Appendix B HTML sanitization (Adopt); Appendix A BUG-004 (Closed) — extends the closure to the remaining 7 sites; Phase 7 discovery: `grep -rn "window\.location\.href" src` returns 7 sites of which 6 are post-BUG-004 unhardened; `grep -rn "spfx-toolkit/lib/utilities/htmlUtils" src` returns 0 hits
   - **Acceptance signal:** `grep -rn "window\.location\.href = " src` returns 0 direct-assignment hits — every navigation flows through `safeNavigate`. `grep -rn "spfx-toolkit/lib/utilities/htmlUtils" src` returns ≥1 hit. Local `sanitizeSummaryHtml` deleted from `documentTitleUtils.ts`. Unit test in `tests/utils/safeNavigate.test.ts` covers (a) `https://` allowed, (b) `/` relative allowed, (c) `javascript:` rejected, (d) `data:` rejected, (e) empty / null rejected.

   - **Acceptance signal:** `README.md` exists at the repo root and links to all five core admin docs + the GitHub Releases page. `grep -n "SPFx 1\.21\|gulp " CLAUDE.md` returns 0 hits. `docs/admin-guide.md:221-226` Manager defaults table matches the shipped manifest values byte-for-byte. `docs/provisioning-guide.md:131-132` accurately describes the automatic retention sweep. `grep -n "Toast" CLAUDE.md` returns 0 hits in the components-used tables. `grep -n "knowledgeBase\|hubSearch\|policySearch" CLAUDE.md` returns 0 hits in the Sprint 4 backlog list (the three are shipped per T4 Current State).

6. **WCAG 2.1 AA top-10 baseline + axe-core CI gate**
   - **Description:** Targeted accessibility baseline pass — top-10 surface gaps surfaced by Journey A/B and Appendix A, NOT an exhaustive WCAG audit. Three artifacts: (a) **Close A11Y-004 + A11Y-005** (Still-Open per Appendix A) — replace the `<div role="radiogroup">` mode toggle at `SpSearchBox.tsx:736` with a semantic `<fieldset>` + `<legend>` (A11Y-004); add `aria-describedby` to the scope selector `Dropdown` at `SpSearchBox.tsx:729` linking to a hidden description element (A11Y-005). (b) **Add `prefers-reduced-motion` respect** in shared SCSS — wrap all `transition` / `animation` / `@keyframes` rules across the 6 `.module.scss` files that use them (`SpSearchBox.module.scss`, `SpSearchVerticals.module.scss`, `SpSearchManager.module.scss`, `DebugPanel.module.scss`, `SpSearchResults.module.scss`, `SpSearchFilters.module.scss` — verified by `grep -l "transition\|@keyframes\|animation"`) in `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference)` or set transition `none` in the reduce branch. Coordinates with T1.D9 — Foundations ships the SCSS infrastructure (a shared `src/styles/motion.scss` mixin), T1.D9 applies it surface-by-surface. (c) **Add axe-core CI gate** — install `axe-core` + `@axe-core/playwright` (or jest-axe for jsdom) as devDependencies; add `tests/a11y/smokeAxe.test.ts` exercising the four most-trafficked render shapes (Search Box mounted, Results in List layout, Filters panel open, Detail panel open); fail CI on any new violation. (d) **Publish `docs/accessibility.md`** with a WCAG 2.1 AA conformance statement scoped to the surfaces axe-core covers, the known limitations (no manual screen-reader pass on file; cite the surfaces left for v1.1+), and the keyboard-only navigation policy (Tab order, focus visible, skip-to-content, Esc-to-close panel). Single deliverable because all four sub-items consume the same a11y-review attention budget and the conformance statement (d) requires (a)+(b)+(c) to be true.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (a) T1 differentiator (Appendix C "Accessibility (WCAG 2.1 AA, keyboard, ARIA)" graded Worse only because SP Search lacks a published conformance statement — fixing that flips the grade) and (e) the audience-profile rule "any SPFx tenant" — enterprise procurement reviews ask for a conformance statement in the first 30 minutes. Closes A11Y-004 + A11Y-005 against the Foundations surface. Default-up tier per the effort rule (design + impl + a11y review).
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** none. T1.D9 takes a downstream cross-track dep — Foundations ships the SCSS infrastructure (motion mixin) + axe-core CI gate; T1.D9 surface-by-surface application + screenshots consumes both. Coordinate sequencing in Sprint 5.
   - **Source:** Appendix A A11Y-004 (Still-Open); Appendix A A11Y-005 (Still-Open); Appendix C "Accessibility (WCAG 2.1 AA, keyboard, ARIA)" Worse; spec §4.4 Foundations accessibility baseline scope item; Phase 7 discovery: `grep -rn "prefers-reduced-motion\|prefers-color-scheme" src` returns 0 hits; `grep -rn "FocusTrapZone\|FocusZone" src/webparts` returns 0 hits; no `docs/accessibility.md` exists

7. **Per-web-part bundle size budget + CI breach gate**
   - **Description:** Define and enforce per-web-part bundle size budgets. Three artifacts: (a) **Document the current sizes** in `docs/performance-budgets.md` (new) — table mirrors the Phase 7 inventory: filters 14.75 MB, results 14.50 MB, admin-manager 11.12 MB, manager 11.12 MB, box 8.49 MB, verticals 7.96 MB; lazy chunks DataGrid 14 KB, VersionHistory 440 KB, SearchManager 519 KB, devextreme date-box vendor 1.07 MB, fluentui Dialog vendor 7.10 MB, devextreme-react core 3.53 MB, xlsx 2.50 MB, PnP PeoplePicker 1.91 MB. (b) **Set per-web-part budgets** — initial budgets at 1.5× current size for each web part (filters ≤22 MB, results ≤22 MB, manager/admin-manager ≤17 MB, box ≤13 MB, verticals ≤12 MB); aspirational target column at 50% of current (long-term work to T1+T5+future tracks); both numbers visible in the `.md` so contributors see the gap. Per-web-part budget per the spec §4.4 wording, NOT a single combined-page budget. (c) **CI breach gate** — add `scripts/check-bundle-sizes.js` (Node script) that runs after `heft build --production`, reads `release/assets/*.js` sizes via `fs.statSync`, compares against `config/bundle-budgets.json`, exits non-zero if any web part exceeds its budget. Wire into CI per D8's GitHub Actions workflow. Reports per-web-part actual + budget + delta on every PR. Existing `npm run stats` and `npm run stats:json` scripts (`package.json:24,25`) already invoke `--emit-stats` — the gate consumes the same build output. (d) **Per-web-part attribution dashboard** — extend the script to emit `release/analysis-logs/bundle-sizes.json` with per-web-part top-10 contributing modules (consumes the existing `webpack-bundle-analyzer` devDep at `package.json:79`); CI uploads as a build artifact so reviewers can see which adopted dependency drove a budget breach. **P0 admission rule:** ties to (d) "would prevent install" because today no admin or developer sees the size of what they are shipping; a self-serve tenant on a constrained network (or with a CDN cost concern) will discover the 14.75 MB Filters bundle by experiencing slow first-paint, not by reading any artifact. Without per-web-part attribution every Adopt-class deliverable (T2.D4 Comments, T2.D5 ManageAccess, T2.D9 keyboard shortcuts) ships blind into a budget no one has set; one careless adoption flips the bundle from "very large" to "site-blocking."
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (d) "would prevent install" — bundles 7–14× over SPFx informal guidance (1–2 MB per web part) on a typical four-web-part page produce ~46 MB unminified before lazy chunks. On constrained networks first-paint is uncacheable until the SharePoint CDN populates, and tenant admins on metered connections will block the install. Pairs with the spec audience-profile rule "self-serve any tenant" — the install bar fails at this size with no diagnostic. Default-up tier per the effort rule (design + impl + cross-test against every Adopt deliverable).
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P0
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 8 (CI workflow is the surface the breach gate runs in)
   - **Source:** spec §4.4 Foundations performance budgets scope item; Phase 7 discovery: `find release/assets -name "sp-search-*-web-part.js" -exec ls -la {} +` reports 7.96–14.75 MB per web part; `grep -rn "bundle.*budget\|max.*size\|webpack.*performance" src config` returns 0 hits
   - **Acceptance signal:** `docs/performance-budgets.md` exists with the per-web-part current/budget/aspirational table populated. `config/bundle-budgets.json` exists with the 6 budget values. Running `node scripts/check-bundle-sizes.js` after `heft build --production` exits 0 today and prints a per-web-part actual/budget/delta line; deliberately bumping any web part by importing a 100 KB module without code-splitting causes the script to exit non-zero with a clear "filters: 14.85 MB exceeds 14.80 MB budget by 50 KB" message. CI build artifact `release/analysis-logs/bundle-sizes.json` enumerates the top-10 contributing modules per web part.

8. **CI / release engineering — GitHub Actions workflow + semver + CHANGELOG + .sppkg release artifact**
   - **Description:** Stand up the missing release engineering surface end-to-end. Single PR-shaped change because every sub-item is one file under `.github/workflows/` or one root-level convention file: (a) **`.github/workflows/build.yml`** — runs on PR + main: `npm install`, `npm run type-check` (post-D3), `npm test`, `npm run package`, `node scripts/check-bundle-sizes.js` (post-D7), uploads `sharepoint/solution/sp-search.sppkg` as a build artifact. Matrix over Node 22.14.x per `package.json:5`. (b) **`.github/workflows/release.yml`** — runs on tag push matching `v*`: rebuilds production, publishes the `.sppkg` to GitHub Releases attached to the tag, generates release notes from `CHANGELOG.md` between the previous and current tag. (c) **Semver policy** — adopt SemVer 2.0; document in `docs/release-policy.md`: major bump on breaking property pane / store API changes, minor on new features, patch on bug fixes; `package.json:3` `version` and `config/package-solution.json:6` `solution.version` move in lockstep (current pinned mismatch — `0.0.1` vs `1.0.13.0` — resolves at the next merge; pick `1.0.0` as the v1.0 RC starting point). (d) **`CHANGELOG.md` at the repo root** — Keep-a-Changelog format; pre-populate the historical entries from the audit-fix sweep (BUG-001..BUG-012 closures cite their commit SHAs in Appendix A — convert to a single `## [1.0.0-rc.1] - 2026-05-DD` entry organised by Added / Changed / Fixed / Security). (e) **`.github/PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md`** + `.github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/{bug_report.md,feature_request.md}` — standard templates with sections for affected web part(s), reproduction steps, screenshot, environment metadata. (f) **`CONTRIBUTING.md`** — short contributor guide pointing to `CLAUDE.md` for architecture, the smoke checklist for testing, and the semver policy for versioning. (g) **`.github/dependabot.yml`** — weekly npm dependency updates targeting devDependencies first, with auto-merge disabled (manual review per PR). The 1.5MB-plus PnP / Fluent / DevExtreme tree changes too often to skip Dependabot but too risky to auto-merge. (h) **Tenant app catalog automation hook** — owned by T4.D10, not D8. Foundations.D8 ships only the GitHub Releases / artifact attachment URL that T4.D10 consumes. If T4.D10 lands first, D8 sub-item (h) is a no-op. (Reference: T4.D10 extends `scripts/Deploy-SPSearchSolution.ps1` to consume the GitHub Releases `.sppkg` URL as a `-ReleaseArtifactUrl` parameter, so an admin can `Deploy-SPSearchSolution.ps1 -ReleaseArtifactUrl 'https://github.com/.../v1.0.0/sp-search.sppkg'` and pull the canonical artifact in one command.)
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (e) Journey A Step 12 [Polish] (no published versioning policy or release tag — admins have no canonical thing to install) and (a) T4 differentiator (release engineering is the substrate T4.D10 mpnId fix and T4.D10 tenant catalog automation consume). Without CI building a `.sppkg` against a tagged commit, the audience-profile rule "self-serve any tenant" has no canonical install artifact pointed-to anywhere; admins are reduced to "build it yourself from a feature branch and hope" — which is exactly the failure mode D2's smoke checklist tries to make repeatable. P1 (not P0) only because the manual workaround "build locally, attach to a one-off email" exists; P0 is reserved for D1/D2/D5/D7 which have no workaround.
   - **Effort:** XL with explicit pre-commitment to peel (h) if T4.D10 lands first. (Eight sub-deliverables in one PR-shaped change is the upper bound of the bundling rule; if any sub-item slips, peel into separate PRs as L+M+M+S+S+S+S+S — but the dependency graph between them keeps them together as a "release engineering substrate" PR.)
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 1 (build must produce `.sppkg` before CI can publish it); Deliverable 7 (bundle-size gate is one of the CI steps). T4.D10 takes a downstream cross-track dep — `Deploy-SPSearchSolution.ps1 -ReleaseArtifactUrl` consumer of the GitHub Releases `.sppkg`.
   - **Source:** spec §4.4 Foundations CI / release engineering scope item; Appendix C "Published compatibility matrix" Worse note (PnP v4 publishes one; SP Search ships nothing); Journey A Step 12 [Polish] (no release tag); Phase 7 discovery: `test -d /Users/hemantmane/Development/sp-search/.github` reports "No .github dir"; no `CHANGELOG.md` / `CONTRIBUTING.md` at root; `package.json:3` version pinned at `0.0.1`
   - **Acceptance signal:** `.github/workflows/build.yml` runs on PR — green CI status surfaces in the PR review surface; build artifact `sp-search.sppkg` downloadable from the PR check. Pushing a tag `v1.0.0` triggers `release.yml` and produces a GitHub Releases entry with `sp-search.sppkg` attached and release notes auto-generated from CHANGELOG. `docs/release-policy.md` exists and is referenced from README. `CHANGELOG.md` exists pre-populated with the audit-fix history. `.github/dependabot.yml` opens its first PR within a week of merge.

9. **Telemetry plumbing — opt-in tenant config + transport service + privacy notice surface**
   - **Description:** Foundations-side substrate that T5.D8 (telemetry strategy + emitter shim) and T5.D9 (telemetry-aggregate dashboard) consume. Four artifacts: (a) **Opt-in storage location** — provision a `SearchTelemetryConfig` SP list (single-row, hidden, item-level read for everyone, write for `Members` group) holding `IsEnabled: boolean`, `DestinationEndpoint: string` (HTTPS POST URL), `BatchIntervalSeconds: number` (default 300), `BatchSizeMax: number` (default 50), `PrivacyAcknowledgedBy: string` (admin login), `PrivacyAcknowledgedAt: datetime`. Provisioning script extension to `scripts/Provision-SPSearchLists.ps1`. (b) **Transport service** — `src/libraries/spSearchStore/telemetry/TelemetryTransport.ts` exposing `flush(batch: ITelemetrySignal[]): Promise<void>` (HTTPS POST, exponential backoff on 4xx/5xx, max 3 retries with 2s/4s/8s delays), `schedule(emitter: TelemetryEmitter)` (drives the batching cadence per `BatchIntervalSeconds`), `loadConfig(): Promise<ITelemetryConfig>` (reads the `SearchTelemetryConfig` list once on init and caches; refreshes every 60s). The transport NEVER inspects payload contents — it is purely the wire; T5.D8's `ITelemetrySignal` interface enforces the never-captured field list at compile time. Transport returns immediately when `config.IsEnabled === false`, so the no-op path is the default. (c) **Privacy notice surface** — `docs/privacy-notice.md` (new) describing the "what we collect / what we never collect" lists verbatim per spec §4.3 T5 ("never captured: query text, user identity, result titles, URLs, tenant names, list item content"); the surface ships on the SharePoint admin-center "App information" pane via `solution.metadata.shortDescription` link to the doc URL; T5.D8's "View what we send" Panel deep-links to the same doc anchor. (d) **`SearchTelemetryOptIn` per-user consent list** — separate from (a)'s config list; tracks per-user opt-in events with the anonymized hash schema T5.D9 specifies (`{ConsentTimestamp, ConsentVersion, AnonHash}` where `AnonHash = SHA-256(tenantId + userPrincipalName + 'sp-search-telemetry-v1') -> first 8 chars`). T5.D9 reads the opt-in count from this list to compute the "Telemetry coverage: X% of users opted in" card. **The deliverable does not pick a destination** — the destination is admin-configured per (a), so the same plumbing supports Application Insights, Azure Monitor, custom HTTPS endpoint, or a tenant-internal logger. **Foundations does NOT define which signals exist** — that is T5.D8's `ITelemetrySignal` schema. Foundations ships the wire and the storage; T5 ships the schema and the consumer. **Destination configuration UI:** admin reaches the SearchTelemetryConfig list via a property-pane field on the Admin Manager (T4.D6 — added to T4.D6's admin-only property pane page) OR via a clickable link in the Pre-Flight tab (T4.D9). Cross-track coordination required: T4.D6 OR T4.D9 must surface the destination URL field; without that surface, the list is admin-edit-only at v1.0.
   - **Why it matters:** Ties to (b) security and (e) the audience-profile rule "self-serve any tenant" — tenant-wide telemetry without explicit tenant-config storage means admins cannot disable, audit, or change the destination after install. Pairs with T5.D8 (no schema → no signals to wire) and T5.D9 (no transport → no aggregate dashboard). The "without Foundations transport, T5.D8 ships in degraded form" wording in T5 Effort Total is the contract this deliverable satisfies.
   - **Effort:** L
   - **Priority:** P1
   - **Depends on:** Deliverable 5 (privacy-notice doc lives in the broader docs surface this PR introduces); T5.D8 (Foundations supplies transport + storage + privacy notice; T5.D8 supplies the schema + emitter + property pane — coordinate so neither ships ahead of the other into a half-wire state). T5.D8 + T5.D9 reciprocate.
   - **Source:** spec §4.4 Foundations telemetry plumbing scope item; T5 Current State (B) "Telemetry — what exists today: Nothing"; T5.D8 dependency line names "Foundations telemetry plumbing"
   - **Acceptance signal:** `SearchTelemetryConfig` SP list provisions on first run of the extended `Provision-SPSearchLists.ps1`. Setting `IsEnabled=true` + `DestinationEndpoint=https://...` in the list and opting in via T5.D8's property pane toggle — the transport flushes a batch of T5.D8's `ITelemetrySignal[]` to the configured endpoint within `BatchIntervalSeconds`; verified via the T5.D2 Network tab showing an outbound `kind: 'telemetryFlush'` row. Setting `IsEnabled=false` — flush is a no-op (no network call recorded). `docs/privacy-notice.md` exists and is referenced from README + admin-guide + T5.D8's "View what we send" Panel. `SearchTelemetryOptIn` list accepts an opt-in row with the SHA-256 hash schema; querying the list returns count without exposing any per-user identifier.

12. **Bundle reduction sweep — Filters + Results + Manager web parts to ≤ initial budget (≤ 1.5× current sizes as Sprint 5 starting point)**
    - **Description:** D7 defines the budgets and the CI breach gate, but defining a budget at 1.5× current sizes still leaves the smallest web part (Verticals at 7.96 MB) ~4× over SPFx informal guidance and the Filters bundle (14.75 MB) ~7× over. The actual reduction work to bring web parts toward the informal 1–2 MB guidance has no other home; without this deliverable, D7's CI gate freezes the install-blocking sizes in place. Three artifacts: (a) **Tree-shaking audit per web part** — for each of Filters (14.75 MB), Results (14.50 MB), Manager + Admin Manager (11.12 MB each), Box (8.49 MB), Verticals (7.96 MB), produce a `webpack-bundle-analyzer` HTML output (consumes the existing `webpack-bundle-analyzer` devDep at `package.json:79`) and check the per-web-part HTML into the PR. Surface the top-10 contributing modules per web part and identify barrel imports / non-tree-shakable dependencies. Coordinates with D7's `release/analysis-logs/bundle-sizes.json` per-web-part attribution dashboard. (b) **Lazy-load remaining heavy DevExtreme components not already lazy** — DataGrid is already `React.lazy()` per the architecture rules; sweep the rest of `devextreme-react/*` direct imports (TagBox, DateRangeBox per CLAUDE.md "lightweight components" allowance — keep direct; FilterBuilder, TreeView, Form, Pivot — push to lazy). Audit each per-web-part bundle for a `vendors-devextreme-*` chunk and convert direct imports to lazy where the component renders below-the-fold or on-demand (filter row, column chooser, virtual scrolling config UI). (c) **Defer non-critical spfx-toolkit imports** — `Toast / ToastProvider` already not adopted (D5 sub-item (e) drops the stale claim); audit each web part's `spfx-toolkit/lib/components/*` direct imports against the actual render path, and convert any that load on first paint but only render on user action (VersionHistory, FormContainer in Detail Panel) to `createLazyComponent` per CLAUDE.md lazy-load guidance. (d) **PR acceptance criteria** — bundle reduction sweep PR cannot land without `webpack-bundle-analyzer` per-web-part HTML attached AND each of the 6 web parts measurably reduced (no per-web-part bundle larger than 1.5× the pre-sweep size — i.e. Filters ≤22 MB, Results ≤22 MB, Manager / Admin Manager ≤17 MB, Box ≤13 MB, Verticals ≤12 MB; aspirational target column from D7 stays at 50% of pre-sweep, but v1.0 ships at the 1.5× bound). The Sprint 5 starting point is the 1.5× ceiling; subsequent sprints in v1.1+ drive toward the aspirational column. **P0 admission rule:** ties to (d) "would prevent install / build" — the initial budget itself (1.5× current sizes) is 1.5× of install-blocking sizes; even the relaxed budget is launch-relevant because constrained-network tenants block on first-paint at the current sizes and a ≤1.5× ceiling does not relieve that pressure unless paired with this active reduction sweep. D7 alone freezes the bad sizes; D12 is the work that brings them down.
    - **Why it matters:** Ties to (d) "would prevent install" — same admission ground as D7 but D7 ships only the budget definition + CI gate while D12 ships the actual reduction. Without D12, D7's gate locks in the install-blocking sizes; with D12, the sizes measurably drop to the relaxed budget by Sprint 5 close and the gate prevents regression. Pairs with every Adopt-class deliverable (T2.D4 Comments, T2.D5 ManageAccess, T2.D9 keyboard shortcuts) — those deliverables ship into a budget D7 enforces and D12 has actively reduced toward, not into the unbounded 14.75 MB starting point.
    - **Effort:** XL
    - **Priority:** P0
    - **Depends on:** Deliverable 7 (budget definition + CI gate is the surface this deliverable reduces against); Deliverable 8 (CI workflow runs the bundle-analyzer step)
    - **Source:** spec §4.4 Foundations performance budgets scope item; Phase 7 discovery: `find release/assets -name "sp-search-*-web-part.js" -exec ls -la {} +` reports 7.96–14.75 MB per web part, ~4–7× over SPFx informal guidance of 1–2 MB; D7 Description identifies the gap but defers the reduction work
    - **Acceptance signal:** `webpack-bundle-analyzer` per-web-part HTML output checked into PR for each of the 6 web parts. After the sweep merges, `find release/assets -name "sp-search-*-web-part.js" -exec ls -la {} +` reports per-web-part sizes within the 1.5× ceilings (Filters ≤22 MB, Results ≤22 MB, Manager / Admin Manager ≤17 MB, Box ≤13 MB, Verticals ≤12 MB). D7's CI gate (`scripts/check-bundle-sizes.js`) passes against the post-sweep sizes. At least 3 of the 6 web parts show a ≥10% reduction from the pre-sweep baseline (the bigger four are the highest-leverage targets).

13. **Fix Jest harness `ts-jest`/`jest-util` resolution failure for `npm test`**
    - **Description:** Diagnose and fix the `ts-jest` / `jest-util` resolution failure documented in CLAUDE.md Sprint 4 backlog. Today `npx jest` fails to resolve its dependencies (per the in-repo backlog note); without a working test harness, every track's "unit test passes" acceptance signal cannot be verified by CI. Two valid shapes: (a) **Upgrade to Heft test pipeline** — `heft test` is already wired into the current `npm test` command (lint blocked per F-1, but the test infrastructure is there per the SPFx 1.22 / Heft migration `a5f28c1`); align the test harness with the migrated build pipeline so `npm test` runs Heft's Jest invocation against the same `tsconfig.json` the build uses. Verify by adding `tests/store/lifecycle.test.ts` (T3.D9 trail-marker — placeholder smoke test) and confirming it executes. (b) **Restore a working `npx jest` invocation** — pin compatible `ts-jest` / `jest-util` versions in `package.json:devDependencies`; update `jest.config.js` (or create one if missing) to use the SPFx-compatible preset; verify `npx jest tests/store/lifecycle.test.ts` exits 0. Prefer (a) — a single test command (`npm test → heft test`) consolidates the build pipeline and matches the Heft-only direction the 1.22 migration committed to. Document the chosen invocation in `CLAUDE.md` Common Commands section + `docs/release-smoke-checklist.md` (D2). **P0 admission rule:** ties to (d) "would prevent install / build" — without this, every track's "unit test passes" acceptance signal cannot be verified by CI; T3.D9 (lifecycle integration tests, which explicitly depend on this fix per CLAUDE.md Sprint 4 backlog reference) and T5.D2 / D3 / D6 / D7 unit-test acceptance signals all silently invalidate. The "self-serve any tenant" launch profile cannot ship a release artifact whose test gate does not run.
    - **Why it matters:** Ties to (d) "would prevent install / build" — the entire downstream test verification surface is gated on a working Jest. Without this fix, every "acceptance signal" line that says "unit test passes" or "smoke test passes" is unverifiable in CI; reviewers can only spot-check manually. Pairs with T3.D9 (lifecycle integration tests, which the CLAUDE.md Sprint 4 backlog explicitly names as blocked on the harness fix) and the T5 acceptance signals across D2 / D3 / D6 / D7 that all assume `npm test` works. Also unblocks D2's pre-merge regression suite (which today says "with the existing Jest harness" — that existing harness is the broken one).
    - **Effort:** M
    - **Priority:** P0
    - **Depends on:** none (independent diagnosis); coordinates with Deliverable 1 (Heft pipeline lint blocker — both share the same Heft test invocation surface) and Deliverable 3 (type-check script — a working test harness pairs with a working type-check script for the D2 pre-merge regression suite).
    - **Source:** CLAUDE.md Sprint 4 backlog "Fix Jest harness (`ts-jest`/`jest-util` resolution failure)"; T3.D9 dependency line names "Foundations plan Jest harness fix"; T5.D2 / D3 / D6 / D7 unit-test acceptance signals; Phase 7 discovery: `npm test` invokes `heft test` per `package.json` but the harness has been documented broken since Sprint 4 backlog capture
    - **Acceptance signal:** `npx jest tests/store/lifecycle.test.ts` (or the Heft-equivalent `npm test -- tests/store/lifecycle.test.ts`) exits 0 against a fresh checkout. CI workflow per D8 runs the test step on every PR and surfaces pass/fail in the review surface. T3.D9's "lifecycle integration tests pass in CI" acceptance signal becomes verifiable. T5 unit-test acceptance signals across D2 / D3 / D6 / D7 become verifiable.

#### Out of scope for v1.0

- **Exhaustive WCAG 2.1 AA audit beyond the top-10 surface gaps.** Rationale: D6 ships top-10 closure + axe-core CI gate + scoped conformance statement. A full WCAG audit (manual screen-reader pass on every component, every focus path, every error-recovery flow) is XL+ and consumes a full a11y-specialist sprint. The audience-profile rule "self-serve any tenant" is satisfied by axe-covered surfaces + scoped conformance statement + the Still-Open A11Y items closed; the exhaustive audit is v1.1+ once usage data identifies which surfaces matter most.
- **Source-mapped production builds.** Rationale: SPFx production builds typically ship without sourcemaps to keep `.sppkg` size down (D7's bundle budgets would tighten further if sourcemaps shipped). Source-mapped stack traces in T5.D3 Errors tab are explicitly OOS for the same reason. Ship line-numbered minified frames; document the limitation in T5.D3's Errors tab header.
- **Heft webpack-extension framework standardization (replace `fast-serve/webpack.extend.js` + `config/spfx-customize-webpack.js` with one shared module).** Rationale: today the webpack patch lives in two places (`config/spfx-customize-webpack.js` for production via `config/heft.json` SPFx integration; `fast-serve/webpack.extend.js` for fast-serve dev mode). Both files are stable and edit-rare. Consolidating into one module would touch the migration surface D2 just stabilised; defer until a third consumer materializes (e.g. a separate test-bundle Webpack pass).
- **Window-key namespace consolidation under a single `window.__sp_search__` object.** Rationale: T3 Out of Scope item 7 ("Window-key namespace consolidation") explicitly defers this to v1.1+; Foundations does not re-litigate. The existing `__sp_search_*` prefix is stable; consolidation is a 1-time migration cost with no observed conflict in the wild.
- **`spfx-toolkit` published-version migration (replace the `file:../spfx-toolkit` link in `package.json:54` with a real npm version).** Rationale: Appendix B Notes column for the toolkit version row explicitly defers the published-version migration ("converting that to a published version is itself a Foundations follow-up, not a Phase 2 deliverable"). Today the local file link is what makes the toolkit Adopt-class deliverables (T2.D4 Comments, T2.D5 ManageAccess) shippable in a single release cycle; cutting to npm requires the toolkit to publish a stable 1.0 first, which is its own gating event. Defer to v1.1.
- **Source-control migration (Git → other) or repo split (per-web-part repos).** Rationale: out of audience-profile scope at v1.0; the single-repo / single-`.sppkg` model is the SPFx convention and matches PnP Modern Search v4. Repo split is a different product shape; defer indefinitely.
- **Public docs site (Docusaurus / VitePress) replacing `docs/*.md`.** Rationale: D5's README + the existing `docs/*.md` set covers the spec §4.4 Foundations docs scope item ("minimum viable docs") at v1.0. A docs site adds deploy-target + per-PR preview infrastructure that exceeds the audience-profile bar. Re-evaluate at v1.1 once the docs surface stabilises and contributor count justifies the toolchain investment.
- **Audience-targeting per web part (Foundations-adjacent parity item).** Rationale: Appendix C "Audience targeting (per-web-part visibility)" graded Worse — PnP exposes audience targeting on every web part; SP Search relies on SP page-level targeting only. This is a property-pane scope item that lives more naturally in T4 than Foundations; capture as v1.1 unless a tenant explicitly blocks on it.

##### Coverage walk (spec §4.4 Foundations subject area → mapping)

- **Security hardening (BUG-004 sweep, HTML sanitization, CSP-friendliness, `window.location.href` + `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` review)** → D4 (HTML sanitizer adopt + 7-site `window.location.href` sweep into shared `safeNavigate` helper); CSP-friendliness today is satisfied by SPFx page-level CSP inheritance and is not a deliverable per spec audience-profile (no admin-configurable CSP surface in SP Search). T2.D3 (saved-search JSON schema validation, SEC-004) covers the input-side that pairs with D4's output-side; cross-tracked.
- **SPFx 1.22 / Heft migration completion (verify nothing regressed, smoke checklist, merge criteria)** → D2 (smoke checklist + pre-merge regression suite + squash-merge + release tag); D1 + D3 are gating fixes (lint blocker + type-check script) that the smoke checklist requires; D5 (CLAUDE.md gulp / 1.21 sweep) lands in the same PR or immediately after.
- **Accessibility baseline (WCAG 2.1 AA, keyboard, screen reader, focus, contrast, ARIA, motion-reduction)** → D6 (top-10 close: A11Y-004 + A11Y-005 + `prefers-reduced-motion` infrastructure + axe-core CI gate + `docs/accessibility.md` conformance statement); T1.D9 takes the surface-by-surface application as a downstream cross-track; exhaustive WCAG audit Out of Scope item 1.
- **CI / release engineering (versioning, `.sppkg` build pipeline, smoke tests, release checklist, changelog)** → D8 (single PR-shaped substrate: `.github/workflows/{build,release}.yml` + semver `docs/release-policy.md` + `CHANGELOG.md` + PR/Issue templates + `CONTRIBUTING.md` + Dependabot + Tenant catalog automation hook owned by T4.D10); D2's smoke checklist consumes the build workflow; D11 metadata cleanup rides along; D13 (Jest harness fix) makes the CI test step real — without it the build workflow runs an unverifiable test gate; T4.D10 reciprocates on tenant-catalog automation
- **Documentation (README → docs site decision, top-level README, per-web-part config, scenario gallery, troubleshooting/FAQ, contributing)** → D5 (README + CLAUDE.md gulp/1.21 sweep + admin-guide Manager defaults + provisioning-guide retention + drop stale Toast claim + drop shipped-presets-as-Sprint-4-backlog claim); D8 ships `CONTRIBUTING.md` + PR/Issue templates; D9 ships `docs/privacy-notice.md`; T2.D12 ships `docs/end-user-guide.md` (cross-tracked); per-web-part config reference + scenario gallery + troubleshooting / FAQ Out of Scope item 7 (deferred to v1.1+ docs site)
- **Telemetry plumbing (opt-in only, query timing, error rates, NEVER queries / PII, admin enable/disable, storage location)** → D9 (opt-in storage `SearchTelemetryConfig` list + `TelemetryTransport.ts` HTTPS POST with backoff + `docs/privacy-notice.md` + `SearchTelemetryOptIn` per-user consent list); T5.D8 ships the schema + emitter shim + property pane that consumes D9; T5.D9 ships the aggregate dashboard view that consumes both.
- **Performance budgets (define + enforce per-web-part, document current, CI breach check)** → D7 (`docs/performance-budgets.md` current/budget/aspirational table + `config/bundle-budgets.json` + `scripts/check-bundle-sizes.js` CI breach gate + per-web-part attribution `release/analysis-logs/bundle-sizes.json`); D12 (active reduction sweep — tree-shaking audit + lazy-load heavy DevExtreme + defer non-critical spfx-toolkit + per-web-part `webpack-bundle-analyzer` HTML in PR); D8 (CI workflow is the surface the breach gate runs in)

##### Effort total

**13 deliverables (6 P0 / 6 P1 / 1 P2)**: P0 = D1 (S) + D2 (L) + D5 (M) + D7 (L) + D12 (XL) + D13 (M); P1 = D3 (S) + D4 (M) + D6 (L) + D8 (XL) + D9 (L) + D10 (S); P2 = D11 (M). Effort tier midpoints (S ≤ 4h ≈ 0.5d; M = ½–1d, midpoint 0.75d; L = 1–3d, midpoint 2d; XL > 3d, midpoint 4d). **Effort total: ~21 dev-days midpoint** (4×L + 2×XL + 3×M + 4×S = 8 + 8 + 3 + 2 = 21d midpoint; honest range 16–30d). Range driver: D8's XL bundle could split into separate PRs if any sub-item slips (workflows + semver + CHANGELOG + templates + Dependabot + automation hook); D7's CI breach gate slips if the `webpack-bundle-analyzer` integration produces noisy per-PR diffs; D12's bundle reduction sweep is the largest single-PR effort and may peel into per-web-part PRs if individual reductions hit non-tree-shakable surfaces. P0 admission rule (each P0 ties to a/b/c/d/e per spec §6): D1 ties (d) "would prevent install / build" — `npm run package` halts at lint with no `.sppkg` produced; D2 ties (d) "would prevent install" — admins cloning `main` get the prior 1.21 + gulp chain, no canonical install artifact; D5 ties (e) Journey A Step 12 [Confusion] (no top-level README) + Journey A Step 1 [Blocker] secondary (CLAUDE.md gulp drift); D7 ties (d) "would prevent install" — bundles 7–14× over SPFx informal guidance produce ~46 MB unminified per typical four-web-part page, install-blocking on constrained networks; D12 ties (d) "would prevent install / build" — the initial budget itself (1.5× current sizes) is 1.5× of install-blocking sizes; even the relaxed budget is launch-relevant because constrained-network tenants block on first-paint at the current sizes and only an active reduction sweep brings them toward the SPFx informal 1–2 MB guidance; D13 ties (d) "would prevent install / build" — without a working Jest harness, every track's "unit test passes" acceptance signal cannot be verified by CI (T3.D9 + T5.D2/D3/D6/D7 silently invalidate). D3 (type-check script) held P1 because the workaround `npx tsc --noEmit` is one command away. D4 (HTML sanitizer + window.location.href) held P1 because no new exposure has been demonstrated in the 7 unhardened sites (admin-configured properties, not user-typed). D6 (a11y baseline) held P1 because the conformance statement is a launch quality lift not a launch blocker. D8 (CI/release engineering) held P1 because the manual workaround "build locally, attach to email" exists. D9 (telemetry plumbing) held P1 because no shipped feature consumes it without T5.D8 + T5.D9 also landing. D10 (`webApiPermissionRequests`) held P1 because the workaround is documented (`admin-guide.md:240-242`). D11 (mpnId / version alignment) held P2 because cosmetic only at install time; rides along with D2's release tag; bumped from S to M to reflect the org-policy decision component.

### Appendix A — March 22 Audit Reconciliation

**Source:** `docs/archive/sp-search-comprehensive-audit-2026-03-22.md`
**Commits inspected since 2026-03-22:** 26 commits across `feat/spfx-1.22-heft-migration` and `main` (the bulk of the audit-fix work landed on 2026-03-22 itself, after the prior audit was authored).

#### Prior audit count note

The prior audit's two summary statistics disagree with each other and with the per-section enumeration:

| Source | Stated total |
|--------|--------------|
| §1 Executive Summary prose ("12 critical/high + 23 medium + 18 low") | 53 |
| §1 Category table totals (7C + 10H + 26M + 20L) | 63 |
| Per-section heading enumeration (this Appendix) | **54** |

This Appendix uses the per-section enumeration as the source of truth. The 54-finding count is derived from: 12 BUG-NNN (§2) + 8 MISS-NNN (§3) + 8 INC-NNN (§4) + 4 SEC (§5; SEC-001 is a cross-reference to BUG-004 and is not double-counted) + 6 PERF (§6) + 6 A11Y (§7) + 7 UX (§8) + 3 ARCH (§9) = 54. The Per-WebPart Summary tables in §10 and the Priority Fix Matrix in §11 use overlapping aggregations and are not separate findings.

Cross-references are track-level only at this stage (T1–T5 / Foundations). Phase 8.1 will tighten these to specific Roadmap IDs.

| SEC-004 | SearchState JSON not schema-validated on restore | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/SavedSearchList.tsx:76,163` parses saved-search state with `JSON.parse` followed by a typed cast and try/catch only — no schema check against `IActiveFilter` shape. Tampered JSON could poison the store. | Foundations |
| PERF-002 | KQL completion scans all schema on every keystroke | Medium | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchBox/kql/KqlCompletionProvider.ts:71-117` linear loop over `schema[]` with `.toLowerCase()` per property per keystroke. No pre-indexed lowercase map. | T2 |
| PERF-004 | Custom `useStoreState` hook verbose shallow comparison | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/SpSearchResults.tsx:188-207` still hand-compares 18 fields. Adding a new store field requires updating the comparator — maintenance risk persists. | T1 |
| PERF-005 | DataGrid color hash runs per-row per-render | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/DataGridContent.tsx:92-104` `getInitialsColor` recomputes per call; no per-name memoization. | T1 |
| PERF-006 | Suggestion `mergeSuggestionsByPriority` creates new Set per call | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchBox/components/SpSearchBox.tsx:33` allocates `new Set<string>()` on every call (5–6 per keystroke when multiple providers are enabled). | T2 |
| A11Y-004 | Mode toggle buttons use `div` instead of `fieldset` | Medium | Still-Open | Verified: `SpSearchBox.tsx:736` `<div className={styles.kqlModeToggle} role="radiogroup" aria-label="Query input mode">`. ARIA role applied but DOM element is still a div, not semantic `<fieldset>` + `<legend>`. | Foundations |
| A11Y-005 | Scope selector missing `aria-describedby` | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `SpSearchBox.tsx:729` Dropdown only sets `ariaLabel="Search scope"`. No linked description text element. | Foundations |
| UX-003 | Query builder no visual confirmation on apply | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchBox/components/QueryBuilder.tsx` has no toast/notification on apply; only inline KQL preview updates. The search executes silently. | T2 |
| UX-004 | Vertical tab switching clears all filters | Low (by design) | Still-Open | Verified: `src/libraries/spSearchStore/store/slices/verticalSlice.ts:11` `setVertical` resets `activeFilters: []`. Audit explicitly tagged this as "by design" but the friction remains and is not yet documented in any in-product UI. | T2 |
| UX-006 | Health tab missing user/vertical breakdown | Medium | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/ZeroResultsPanel.tsx:32-64` `aggregateEntries` collapses only by query text + vertical (no per-user view). Admins can't distinguish systemic vs. user-specific issues. | T5 |
| UX-007 | Insights CTR not time-weighted | Low | Still-Open | Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/SearchInsightsPanel.tsx` aggregates over the entire window. Comment at `:298` mentions "Daily volume sparkline for trend visibility", but CTR itself is a single window-wide number, not trended week-over-week. | T5 |
| ARCH-002 | Formatter implementation split between store and web part | Low | Still-Open | Verified: formatters exist in BOTH `src/libraries/spSearchStore/formatters/` (registered via `getFilterValueFormatter`) AND `src/webparts/spSearchFilters/formatters/` (`PeopleFilterFormatter.ts`, `BooleanFilterFormatter.ts`, `DateFilterFormatter.ts`, `NumericFilterFormatter.ts`, `TaxonomyFilterFormatter.ts`). Risk of display inconsistencies remains. | Foundations |
| ARCH-003 | Initialization order dependency not enforced | Medium | Still-Open | Verified: `src/libraries/spSearchStore/store/storeRegistry.ts:189` flips `isInitialized = true` and `:191-198` documents the ordering convention in a comment, but nothing programmatically enforces "Results web part calls `initializeSearchContext()` first, then triggers search". | Foundations |
| MISS-004 | Show more/less inconsistent across filter types | Medium | Changed-Form | Partial fix commit `9e26d08` added showMore to TagBox + Dropdown; verified at `src/webparts/spSearchFilters/components/TagBoxFilter.tsx:184`, `DropdownFilter.tsx:146`, `CheckboxFilter.tsx:213`. **Residual gap:** Taxonomy and People filter types still lack a "Show more" affordance — they use type-ahead/tree expand only. | T1 |
| INC-001 | Manual apply mode edge cases | Medium | Changed-Form | Partial fix commit `9c67332` added external-change sync. Verified: `SpSearchFilters.tsx:303-317` syncs pending state with store changes; `:512-523` renders Apply bar. **Residual gap:** No visual count of pending changes (e.g., "3 pending"). The audit's "no visual indicator" point still stands. | T1 |
| INC-007 | Admin Manager is a re-export stub | High | Changed-Form | Fix commit `02c6adc`. Verified: `SpSearchAdminManagerWebPart.ts:16` is `extends SpSearchManagerWebPart`; `onInit` only adds DebugCollector instrumentation. **Residual gap:** behavior is 100% inherited; the only differentiation is preconfigured manifest defaults plus the DebugCollector hook in `onInit`. | T4 |
| SEC-002 | Preview iframe allows scripts | Medium | Changed-Form | Fix commit `c2c1d26` removed `allow-forms`. Verified: `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/ResultDetailPanel.tsx:282` sandbox is now `allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups`. **Residual:** `allow-scripts` retained intentionally (WOPI requires it; documented in the inline comment), so the original recommendation to drop `allow-scripts` was rejected. | Foundations |
| UX-005 | Zero-result panel not real-time | Low | Changed-Form | Manual `Refresh` button added (`src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/ZeroResultsPanel.tsx:126-128,168`). **Residual:** No subscription to live history writes; admin must click Refresh to see new zero-result entries. | T5 |
| BUG-006 | Debounce timer executes with stale state snapshot | High | Obsolete | Design changed. `SearchOrchestrator.ts:203-204` comment explicitly states `_executeSearch()` reads fresh state via `this._store.getState()` at call time, so changes during the debounce window are *intended* to be captured. The audit framed this as a bug; the resolved design treats fresh-state reads as the contract. | T3 |

### Appendix B — spfx-toolkit Integration Map

This appendix maps newly-shipped `spfx-toolkit` capabilities (since SP Search last integrated) to candidate adoption points in SP Search. It drives Phase 7 / per-track planning, not direct execution — every "Adopt" or "Consider" row should be re-evaluated against the relevant per-track plan before any implementation work begins.

**Toolkit version inspected:** `1.0.0-alpha.1` at `/Users/hemantmane/Development/spfx-toolkit`, commits `1edde9d..920cddb` (2026-01-03 → 2026-04-09; 28 commits inspected via `git log --since='2026-01-01'`). SP Search currently consumes the toolkit via the local file link `"spfx-toolkit": "file:../spfx-toolkit"` in `package.json` — converting that to a published version is itself a Foundations follow-up, not a Phase 2 deliverable.

| Capability | Status | Where it would land in SP Search | Effort | Differentiator | Notes |
|------------|--------|-----------------------------------|:------:|:--------------:|-------|
| **HTML sanitization** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/utilities/htmlUtils/sanitizeHtml`, commit `8e9b311`) | Adopt | `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/documentTitleUtils.ts:155` (`sanitizeSummaryHtml`) — replace local sanitizer used at `ListLayout.tsx:69` `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` | S | Foundations | Toolkit sanitizer has explicit `ALLOWED_TAGS` + `LINK_ATTRIBUTES` allowlists and `isSafeUrl` predicate; replacing the local implementation reduces XSS surface and centralizes the policy. Pairs naturally with the BUG-004 fix sweep called out in the spec §4.4 Foundations track. |
| **Browser storage utilities** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/utilities/browserStorage`, commit `8e9b311`) | Adopt | `SearchManagerService.ts:729,742,764,818` (cleanup-key timestamp), `SchemaService.ts:185,197,206,214` (schema cache), `SpSearchBox.tsx` `SCOPE_STORAGE_KEY` (`:112,144-161,428-432`), `DataGridContent.tsx` (column prefs) | M | Foundations | Centralizes try/catch + availability detection (`isBrowserStorageAvailable`) currently re-implemented inline at 4+ sites. Reduces risk of `QuotaExceededError` regressions called out in `MEMORY.md` PnPjs caching note. |
| **Comments component** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/components/Comments`, commits `523be2a`, `7c798f4`, `434d9ad`, `0aa4dda`, `920cddb`) | Adopt | `src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/ResultAnnotations.tsx` — extend the current tag-only annotation row with a comments thread per saved search / collection item | L | T2 | Toolkit ships hooks (`useComments`, `useCommentInput`, `useCommentSearch`), classic/chat/compact/timeline layouts, @mention search backed by Graph/PeoplePicker, and #link with DocumentLink preview. Directly satisfies a v1.0 productivity differentiator (annotations + collaboration on saved searches / collections). Prerequisite: target SP list with `Comments` field; verify list provisioning script covers it. |
| **ManageAccess panel** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/components/ManageAccess`, commits `2b693b3`, `7cf9186`, `1edde9d`) | Adopt | `src/webparts/spSearchManager/components/ShareSearchDialog.tsx` — replace ad-hoc share-to-users tab with `ManageAccessPanel`, surfacing existing permissions, role assignments, and removal | M | T2 | Current dialog only adds users; cannot view/revoke. ManageAccess covers principal listing + permission level changes + removal in one panel, matching the "personal vs shared library boundaries" deliverable in spec §4.3 T2. Pairs with the Still-Open BUG-012 evidence (`SearchManagerService.ts:1349-1408`) for a unified sharing UX. |
| **CssLoader compatibility aliases** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/utilities/CssLoader`, commits `5ee7cfa`, `7d943a7`) | Consider | `gulpfile.js` `additionalConfiguration` (sp-css-loader exclusion pattern; CLAUDE.md rule #9) | S | Foundations | SP Search currently solves the external-CSS-with-binary-fonts problem at the webpack-config level. Toolkit's CssLoader is an `SPComponentLoader.loadCss`-based runtime loader for Style Library files — solves a different problem. Could simplify admin-managed theming overrides if SP Search exposes one, but no current admin theming surface. Re-assess after T1 (Modern UI Quality) settles its theming story. |
| **FormErrorSummary + FormContext fixes** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/components/spForm`, commits `9ec580e`, `12baab6`, `a5f3ad3`) | Consider | Property pane forms (e.g., `propertyPaneControls/SchemaHelperControl.tsx`) and Search Manager edit dialogs | M | T4 | SP Search property panes currently use plain Fluent UI controls and PnP property controls — not the toolkit `spForm` stack. Adopting `spForm` for edit-mode validation lint (a stated T4 deliverable) is a larger design decision; the recent fixes only matter once `spForm` is the chosen form host. Defer the framework decision to the T4 plan. |
| **ConflictDetector** (`spfx-toolkit/lib/components/ConflictDetector`, commit `df40048`) | Consider | `SearchManagerService.ts` saved-search and collection update paths; `ResultAnnotations.tsx` annotation edits | L | T2 | Saved searches and collections are list items that two admins or the same user across two devices could edit concurrently. ConflictDetector wraps SP ETag checks with a hooks/context API. Worthwhile only if user research shows real concurrent-edit pain; otherwise the optimistic-overwrite default is acceptable for v1.0. Defer scoping to T2 plan. |
| **GroupUsersPicker + GroupViewer fixes** (commits `b43e639`, `a5f3ad3`, `0c8c914`) | Consider | `ShareSearchDialog.tsx` "Share to Users" tab (currently uses PnP PeoplePicker) | S | T2 | If ManageAccess adoption (above) lands first, GroupUsersPicker becomes a sub-decision inside that panel. Re-evaluate only if ManageAccess is rejected. |
| **VersionHistory restyling** (commits `1edde9d`, prior consumption already in `ResultDetailPanel.tsx:7`) | Adopt | `src/webparts/spSearchResults/components/ResultDetailPanel.tsx` — pull the latest VersionHistory styles automatically via existing import | S | T1 | Already consumed; this is a free upgrade once the toolkit version is bumped or re-built locally. SharePoint-native theme alignment supports the T1 Modern UI Quality theming-consistency deliverable. No code change required beyond `npm run build` of the linked toolkit. |
| **UserPersona / userPhotoHelper deduplication** (commits `9c72ec0`, prior consumption in `ResultDetailPanel.tsx:7`, `ListLayout.tsx:4`, `DocumentTitleHoverCard.tsx:8`) | Adopt | Existing UserPersona consumption sites; no new wiring | S | T1 | Performance + correctness improvement to a component already in use across three layouts. Free upgrade on next toolkit rebuild. |
| **NoteHistory dedup / cache-busting** (`spFields/SPTextField/NoteHistory.tsx`, commit `07d1196`) | No Fit | n/a — SP Search does not consume `spFields` or `SPDynamicForm` | — | — | SP Search has no Note field UI; relevant only if a future admin form adopts `SPDynamicForm`. |
| **SPDynamicForm + spFields suite** (`SPLookupField`, `SPTaxonomyField`, etc., commit `13dd811`) | No Fit | n/a — SP Search uses property pane + custom edit dialogs, not toolkit dynamic forms | — | — | Adopting `SPDynamicForm` would be a much larger architectural shift than v1.0 warrants. Tracked under T4 only if a future "admin schema editor" surface materializes. |
| **SPListItemAttachments** (existing) | No Fit | n/a — saved searches and collections do not carry attachments | — | — | No use case in current data model. |

### Appendix C — PnP Modern Search v4 Parity Scorecard

This appendix grades SP Search feature-by-feature against PnP Modern Search v4 (latest stable v4.21.0, released 2026-04-16). It informs **positioning, not a forced parity backlog** — per spec §3 Non-Goals, missing PnP features are deliverables only if they tie to a stated differentiator (T1–T5). PnP v4's documentation surface (per its docs nav: Search Box, Search Results, Search Filters, Search Verticals, Extensibility) is used as the canonical structure to avoid omissions, extending the existing alignment notes in `docs/pnp-modern-search-alignment.md` rather than duplicating them. Grades are: **Better** (SP Search exceeds, citing the SP Search file/feature), **Parity** (equivalent), **Worse** (SP Search has it but inferior, citing the gap), **Missing** (not in SP Search, citing where in PnP it lives).

#### Scorecard

| Area | PnP v4 Feature | Grade | SP Search Equivalent | Notes |
|------|----------------|:-----:|----------------------|-------|
| Search Box | Free-text query input + placeholder + clear | Parity | `src/webparts/spSearchBox/components/SpSearchBox.tsx` | Both ship the basic input, placeholder, and clear-on-Esc. |
| Search Box | Query suggestions (multiple providers, configurable per-group count) | Better | `src/libraries/spSearchStore/providers/{RecentSearchProvider,TrendingQueryProvider,ManagedPropertyProvider,QuerySuggestionProvider,QuickResultsSuggestionProvider}.ts`; suggestion registry in `SuggestionProviderRegistry.ts` | SP Search ships 5 providers vs PnP's 1 built-in (SP Static); registry pattern allows late registration; AbortController cancellation per BUG-011 fix; `aria-activedescendant` per A11Y-002 fix. |
| Search Box | Query input transformation (token-aware template) | Worse | `SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts` exposes `queryInputTransformation` property; `SearchOrchestrator.ts:97,115,151,704-706` watches it for re-search | MISS-001 Still-Open (Sprint 4 backlog): property is surfaced and triggers re-search but the broader transformation pipeline is not fully applied end-to-end (per Appendix A). |
| Search Box | Search-in-new-page (URL fragment or parameter) | Parity | `SpSearchBox.tsx:336-343` validates `newPageUrl` then navigates | XSS-hardened post BUG-004 (`https://`/`http://`/`/` only). |
| Search Box | KQL editor with autocomplete + validation | Better | `src/webparts/spSearchBox/kql/{KqlInput,KqlParser,KqlCompletionProvider}.tsx`; mode toggle in `SpSearchBox.tsx:736` | PnP v4 has no first-class KQL authoring surface; SP Search ships quote-aware parser (INC-003 fix), validation panel (INC-002 fix), and visual Query Builder (`QueryBuilder.tsx`). |
| Search Box | Configurable scopes / result sources | Better | `SpSearchBoxWebPart.ts:385-` `searchScopes` PropertyFieldCollectionData; persisted to localStorage per `SpSearchBox.tsx:112,144-161,428-432` | PnP exposes a single result-source-id property; SP Search ships scope selector + per-scope KQL path + persistence (MISS-005 + MISS-008 closed). |
| Search Results | Data sources (SharePoint Search, Microsoft Search, Azure AI Search, custom) | Worse | `providers/SharePointSearchProvider.ts`, `providers/GraphSearchProvider.ts`; `ISearchDataProvider` interface | SP Search ships 2 built-in providers (SharePoint + Graph); PnP v4 ships 4+ (SP, MS Search, Azure AI Search, custom via `IDataSource`). Per-vertical `dataProviderId` routing (Sprint 3) partially mitigates but Azure AI Search and standalone Microsoft Search are absent. See https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/usage/search-results/ |
| Search Results | Result layouts catalogue | Better | 6 layouts: `ListLayout.tsx`, `CompactLayout.tsx`, `CardLayout.tsx`, `GalleryLayout.tsx`, `PeopleLayout.tsx`, `DataGridLayout.tsx` (DevExtreme-backed) | PnP ships List/Cards/Tiles/Debug + custom-layout extensibility. SP Search adds DataGrid (column chooser, virtual scroll, CSV+XLSX export, persisted prefs per Sprint 3 + MISS-003 fix) and Graph-backed People layout — both stronger than PnP's Handlebars equivalents on the Modern UI Quality + Admin Experience differentiators. |
| Search Results | Handlebars templating | Missing | n/a — SP Search uses React + cell renderers (`cellRenderers/*`) | PnP v4 layouts are Handlebars + web components (https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/extensibility/templating/). SP Search's React-component model is a deliberate paradigm difference, not a gap to close — admins extend via `ILayoutDefinition` + cell renderers, not Handlebars. |
| Search Results | Slots (token-bound result fields) | Missing | n/a — SP Search uses `selectedProperties` array + cell renderer mapping | PnP "slots" let admins declare which managed property maps to title/path/preview/etc. without editing the layout. SP Search's columns config is more direct but lacks the slot abstraction layer. https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/usage/search-results/ |
| Search Results | Tokens (`{searchTerms}`, `{Site.ID}`, `{User.Email}`, etc.) | Parity | `src/libraries/spSearchStore/services/TokenService.ts`; `queryTemplate` defaults to `{searchTerms}` per alignment doc | Token catalogue is comparable per `docs/pnp-modern-search-alignment.md`. |
| Search Results | Sorting (configurable + user-selectable) | Parity | `SpSearchResults.tsx:793` sort dropdown, gated by sortable layouts post UX-001 fix | Sort dropdown hidden for People/Gallery/Card. |
| Search Results | Paging | Parity | `Pagination.tsx`; configurable `pageSize` + `pageRange` per alignment doc | |
| Search Results | Detail / preview panel | Better | `ResultDetailPanel.tsx` with version history, metadata, related docs; iframe sandbox tightened post SEC-002 (Changed-Form) | PnP has no built-in detail panel; admins must hand-author Handlebars hover cards. |
| Search Results | Bulk selection + multi-item actions | Better | `BulkActionsToolbar.tsx`; selection lives in `uiSlice` | PnP has no native bulk actions; admins script via web components. |
| Search Results | Result actions registry (Open/Preview/Share/Pin/Copy/Download/Compare) | Better | `providers/actions/{Open,Preview,Share,Pin,CopyLink,Download,Compare,ExportCsv}Action.ts`; `ActionProviderRegistry` | PnP's action surface is per-template Handlebars; SP Search has a typed registry with 8 built-in actions. |
| Search Results | Promoted results / Best Bets | Better | `PromotedResultsBlock.tsx` (client-side, position #0); admin-defined via SharePoint Query Rules per CLAUDE.md Security Rule #5 | PnP v4 has no client-side promoted results block; relies on invisible server-side ranking. |
| Search Filters | Standard refiners (Checkbox, Date Range, Combo/Dropdown, TagBox, People, Taxonomy Tree) | Parity | `CheckboxFilter.tsx`, `DateRangeFilter.tsx` (FQL `range()` per CLAUDE.md Data Rule #5), `DropdownFilter.tsx`, `TagBoxFilter.tsx`, `PeoplePickerFilter.tsx` (`AuthorOWSUSER`), `TaxonomyTreeFilter.tsx` (GP0\|#GUID resolution) | Catalogue maps 1:1 to PnP's Checkbox/Date Range/Combo/People/Hierarchical templates. Show-more still missing for Taxonomy + People per MISS-004 Changed-Form residual. |
| Search Filters | Date interval (relative ranges: today/week/month/year) | Worse | `DateRangeFilter.tsx` supports custom range only | PnP v4 ships pre-canned interval buckets. https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/usage/search-filters/ |
| Search Filters | Extra filter types (Slider numeric, Text, Toggle, Visual builder) | Better | `SliderFilter.tsx`, `TextFilter.tsx`, `ToggleFilter.tsx`, `VisualFilterBuilder.tsx` | None of these have PnP v4 equivalents. |
| Search Filters | Operator between filters (AND/OR) | Worse | `SpSearchFiltersWebPart.ts` exposes `operatorBetweenFilters`; orchestrator watches it (BUG-001 closed) | MISS-002 Still-Open: filter execution path may not consistently apply OR semantics across groups (Appendix A row). |
| Search Filters | Manual apply mode + clear-all | Parity | Apply bar `SpSearchFilters.tsx:512-523`; Clear-All `:483-484` post MISS-006 fix | INC-001 Changed-Form residual: no pending-count indicator. |
| Search Filters | Sticky / persisted filter state across vertical switches | Worse | `verticalSlice.ts:11` `setVertical` clears `activeFilters: []` | UX-004 Still-Open by-design choice; PnP keeps filters across verticals when refiner names match. |
| Search Verticals | Tabs with badge counts, per-vertical query/filters config, responsive overflow | Parity | `SpSearchVerticals.tsx` (Fluent `OverflowSet` per MISS-007 closed); `SpSearchVerticalsWebPart.ts` `verticals` collection | |
| Search Verticals | Per-vertical data source / provider routing | Better | Per-vertical `dataProviderId` routes to `SharePointSearchProvider` or `GraphSearchProvider` (Sprint 3 capability per `MEMORY.md`) | PnP v4 verticals share the parent web part's single data source. |
| Extensibility | Typed extension points (custom data sources, suggestions providers, layouts) | Parity | `ISearchDataProvider`, `ISuggestionProvider`, `ILayoutDefinition` with corresponding registries; suggestion registry intentionally NOT frozen per MEMORY.md note | Paradigm difference — SP Search uses TS interfaces + React; PnP v4 uses `IDataSource`/`IExtensibilityLibrary` + Handlebars. https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/extensibility/ |
| Extensibility | Handlebars helpers, partials, and custom web components | Missing | n/a | PnP v4 layouts are Handlebars + custom HTML web components. SP Search routes the same intent through React composition + cell renderers — deliberate divergence, not a v1.0 deliverable. https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/extensibility/templating/ |
| Extensibility | Custom query modifiers | Worse | `queryInputTransformation` property surfaced but pipeline incomplete (MISS-001) | PnP ships full IQueryModifier interface. https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/extensibility/custom-query-modifier/ |
| Extensibility | Custom Adaptive Cards event handlers | Missing | n/a — SP Search does not render Adaptive Cards | https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/extensibility/custom-event-handlers/ |
| Extensibility | Published compatibility matrix | Worse | No published compatibility matrix; alignment notes touch on it | https://microsoft-search.github.io/pnp-modern-search/extensibility/compatibility-matrix/ |
| Cross-cutting | Search Manager (saved searches, sharing, collections, history, annotations) | Better | `SpSearchManagerWebPart` + `SearchManagerService.ts` (CRUD, item-level perms via `breakRoleInheritance`); `SavedSearchList`, `SearchCollections`, `SearchHistory`, `ShareSearchDialog`, `ResultAnnotations` | PnP v4 has no equivalent — entirely missing on PnP side. Direct T2 differentiator delivery. |
| Cross-cutting | Admin Dashboard (Coverage Stats / Quality Metrics / Health / Insights) | Better | `AdminDashboard.tsx`, `ZeroResultsPanel.tsx`, `SearchInsightsPanel.tsx`, `CoverageStatsService` | PnP has no admin analytics surface. T4 + T5 differentiator delivery. UX-006 / UX-007 are Still-Open polish items. |
| Cross-cutting | Multi-instance isolation via `searchContextId` | Better | `storeRegistry.ts:217` per-context store + `_buildStableUrlPrefix`; `window.__sp_search_context_map__` cross-webpart singleton (CLAUDE.md architecture note); URL namespacing `?ctx1.q=...` | PnP v4 uses Dynamic Data which couples instances; T3 differentiator delivery. |
| Cross-cutting | Debug FAB / DebugPanel (Query/Network/State/Logs/Errors) | Better | `DebugFab.tsx`, `DebugPanel.tsx` | PnP has no in-product diagnostics surface. T5 differentiator delivery. |
| Cross-cutting | Scenario presets (`general`, `documents`, `news`, `people`, `media`, `custom`) | Better | `searchPresets.ts` `SCENARIO_PRESETS`; `_applyScenarioPreset()`; `Search-ScenarioPresets.ps1` | PnP has no preset registry; admins hand-configure each web part. T4 differentiator. |
| Cross-cutting | Theming (Office UI Fabric / Fluent integration) | Parity | Fluent UI v8 throughout; theme-aware CSS variables | Both honour SharePoint section themes. |
| Cross-cutting | Accessibility (WCAG 2.1 AA, keyboard, ARIA) | Worse | A11Y-001/002/003/006 closed; A11Y-004/005 Still-Open | No published WCAG conformance statement on either side; SP Search closed 4 of 6 audit items but has no A11y test pass on file. PnP v4 has no documented A11y baseline either, so the gap is "neither claims AA"; SP Search graded Worse only because it lacks a published conformance statement. Foundations track. |
| Cross-cutting | Mobile responsiveness | Parity | Sprint 3 hardening per `MEMORY.md`: gallery single-column at 399px, overlay backdrop-filter, iOS DataGrid momentum scroll | |
| Cross-cutting | Telemetry (opt-in product signals) | Missing | n/a — no telemetry pipeline | PnP v4 also has no first-class telemetry. SP Search may add opt-in per spec §4.4 Foundations (telemetry plumbing). |
| Cross-cutting | Audience targeting (per-web-part visibility) | Worse | Not implemented as a first-class property | PnP exposes audience targeting on every web part; SP Search relies on SP page-level audience targeting only. |

#### Positioning takeaways

- **SP Search wins on differentiators that PnP v4 doesn't even attempt.** Search Manager (saved/shared/collections/history), Admin Dashboard (Health + Insights), Debug FAB, multi-context isolation via `searchContextId`, scenario presets, KQL editor, and DataGrid layout are all entirely-missing-in-PnP capabilities that anchor T2/T3/T4/T5 differentiators.
- **Filter and refiner catalogue is at parity with one notable gap and one notable strength.** SP Search ships Slider/Text/Toggle and a Visual Filter Builder that PnP doesn't, but lacks PnP's Date Interval (relative-range buckets) — a T1/T4 polish item, easy add.
- **Data source breadth is a real positioning weakness.** PnP v4 ships SharePoint + Microsoft Search + Azure AI Search + custom; SP Search ships SharePoint + Graph only. Per-vertical `dataProviderId` routing softens the gap, but Azure AI Search support is increasingly table stakes for enterprise demos. Decide explicitly whether to invest (T4 deliverable) or document as out-of-scope (Appendix D).
- **Templating paradigm is a deliberate divergence, not a gap to close.** PnP's Handlebars + web components is genuinely more flexible for non-developer admins; SP Search's React + cell renderers + registries is more type-safe and tree-shakable. Document this as a positioning choice in launch materials so prospects don't expect Handlebars.
- **Cross-cutting hygiene (accessibility conformance statement, audience targeting, telemetry) is the area where SP Search is materially behind.** None of these tie to a stated differentiator on their own, but each one fails the "self-serve any tenant" launch bar (spec §3.1) in ways an enterprise procurement review will catch. Foundations track.
